on guiding farmers to destroy some of the cotton seedlings have been quite successful. The Department of Agriculture now hopes that 11,732,000 acres can be reduced this year. According to reports from various places, although cotton prices have risen, farmers are still quick to obey. If the number of acres reduced this year can reach what the Department of Agriculture hopes for at this time, then this year's cotton harvest should be 30% less than in 1931. (National Telegram, 27th)

Plan to Raise Sugar Prices Proposed 19

Washington: With the hope of success in reducing

the planting of cotton, the U.S. Department of Agriculture today began meetings with sugar producers from the United States, Cuba, Puerto Rico, and Honolulu, in an attempt to reduce the planting area and ask them to assist the government in creating a major plan to raise sugar prices. However, representatives of U.S. sugar producers advocated levying full taxes on Cuban sugar and strictly restricting the import of Philippine sugar, and were unwilling to reduce the planting area in their own country and Honolulu. However, under the current circumstances, if the excess sugar is to be sold off and the sugar industry is to be restored to prosperity, the sugar planting acreage must be reduced uniformly in the United States and Honolulu. According to the Agricultural Relief Act, sugar is also listed as a basic commodity, and cotton producers can also receive some benefits as well as those who plant cotton and wheat. (National Telegram, 27th)

Washington: The U.S. Department of Agriculture has proposed that sugar producers in the United States and Honolulu should reduce planting area together with Cuba and Puerto Rico. However, U.S. sugar producers are unwilling to reduce their own planting area and want to restrict the import of other sugar. Therefore, representatives from U.S. sugar producer groups and refining groups today elected a committee to draft a plan for submission to the Department of Agriculture for consideration. (National Telegram, 27th)

Various Subcommittees Begin Adjustment Work 22

(London) Today, the World Economic Conference has begun to engage in the adjustment of the work of various committees and subcommittees. Furthermore, the expert subcommittee on currency issues has today completed its discussion on the issue of cash circulation and the legal minimum limit of gold reserves in various central banks. Britain Proposes Resolution to Reorganize Debt Issue 23

(London) The British delegation this morning submitted a resolution to the drafting committee established in the Economic Committee responsible for studying methods of financial reorganization. The content first acknowledges that the recovery of world commerce depends entirely on the recovery of international loans. The second point is that under the current difficult circumstances, the recovery of international loans is unlikely. According to the British plan, the credit of various debtor countries must be preserved, as it is the first condition for the recovery of international loans. The British proposal continues to say that the various debtor countries are admirable for continuing to fulfill their obligations despite encountering various difficulties. The proposal also states that creditor countries should remove obstacles to allow the free flow of goods, so that the credit of various debtor countries can be preserved and there is no need to worry about the loans made by the creditor countries themselves. The British proposal also states that the rise in world prices is naturally beneficial to various debtor countries. However, before the changes in world prices become clear, we should not hope for a lasting reform of commercial debts. What we should do is only to establish a temporary compromise between creditor countries and debtor countries, and the method should be determined according to the surrounding circumstances of each debt, and should not be rigid. The British proposal finally proposes that an organization be formed by representatives of various foreign bondholders. (Havas, 27th)

Economic Production and Sales Group

Wheat Production Adjustment Issue 24

Opinions of Representatives from Four Countries are Complex

Still Far From Reaching an Agreement

(London) This year's U.S. wheat harvest is expected to be unusually poor due to extreme heat and wind and rain. Therefore, wheat prices have been soaring in recent days, affecting the Economic Conference. Just as representatives from the United States, Argentina, Canada, and Australia were discussing plans to reduce wheat planting area using domestic political programs today, a telegram was received from Chicago that wheat prices had exceeded the gold currency line, which had not been seen for many years. This led to the interruption of the meeting of the four representatives. The Argentine representative stated that restricting the acreage would provoke resistance from farmers at a time when they are hoping for prosperity. When wheat prices are sold for half a dollar per bushel, it is appropriate to reduce the acreage. If it rises to one dollar, another problem will arise. However, the Australian representative is still fully willing to join the agreement to reduce the planting area. The Canadian and American representatives also feel that it is still necessary to implement the acreage reduction movement in order to prevent excessive production in the coming year. The U.S. representative also stated that the U.S. President is still determined to carry out this plan, believing that the impact of one poor harvest is limited and that it is difficult to benefit for a long time. (National Telegram, 27th)

London: The adjustment of wheat production has become a complex issue in the World Economic Conference. The afternoon meeting today continued to discuss this matter. It is believed that the Australian representative, Bruce, has received a telegram from his government, but the content is unknown. It was heard that Mr. Bruce refused to reduce the number of acres of wheat fields at the meeting this morning. At that time, a certain U.S. representative stood up and said that if this matter could not be agreed upon, the United States and Canada would sell about 530 million bushels of excess wheat on the market. Mr. Bruce telegraphed Canberra to ask for new instructions. Currently, the price of wheat in New York has exceeded one dollar. This price means that the provisions of the U.S. Farm Bill to reduce the number of acres of wheat fields will begin to be implemented. This matter has made the conference situation more complicated. The opinion of U.S. observers is that this price is not natural, but it is generally believed that if this price persists, the provisions of the Farm Bill must begin to be implemented.

Concentrate on Overall Planning 25

Subcommittee Drafts Report

Cuban Sugar Proposal Submitted for Discussion

Today's discussion focused on comprehensive planning of production and consumption issues, rather than simply reducing production. Regarding this section, sugar is the first item discussed by the subcommittee. The subcommittee drafted a comprehensive report, advocating that for all major items currently in surplus, both production and sales must be taken into account. All representatives at the meeting agreed that any new plan must obtain the consent of the majority of producers and the willing cooperation of importing countries in order to be effective. All representatives also agreed to the suggestion made by the Dutch representative to organize a special committee of representatives from major sugar producing countries to study the Cuban sugar proposal. Dr. Walter, the German representative, said that the Cuban proposal advocates a ten-year agreement, and he suggested that the term of the agreement should be reduced to three or five years. However, the speakers from the Netherlands, Poland, Peru, and Portugal all agreed to the Cuban plan. (Reuters, 27th)

London: The subcommittee of the Economic Committee of the World Economic Conference, which is discussing production and sales, has established a new draft, stipulating the necessary conditions for the reorganization plan: 1. So-called production should include excess production and inventory. 2. Compromises should include joint production and substitutes. 3. The scope of producing countries should be as broad as possible, that is, all exporting countries should be universally involved, and then non-exporting countries with extremely large production should also be sought to join. 4. Fairness should be sought for producers and consumers, and the cooperation of consumers should be sought as much as possible. 5. The implementation period should be sufficiently long. 6. All relevant countries should be able to implement it. 7. Reorganization plans should be able to adapt to the increase in demand. 8. Reorganization plans should also take into account the internal incentives for countries to clarify production. (Havas, 27th)

Reserves Freedom to Impose Retaliatory Taxes

Foreign Minister Uchida telegraphed Ambassador Matsudaira in the United Kingdom at 4:00 PM this afternoon and handed it to Chairman MacDonald of the Economic Conference, expressing formal acceptance of the truce plan. (Hualianshe, 28th)

Tokyo: The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs simultaneously released the full text of the reservation as follows: 1. Regarding this resolution, the Imperial Government, based on the reservations made or to be made by other governments, does not assume the obligation to promise regarding the measures taken or to be taken. 2. Regardless of whether or not the government participating in this resolution, for all measures taken or to be taken by other governments after May 12, 1932, to raise tariffs and other measures that hinder Japanese trade, the government's necessary measures taken for defense will not be hindered by the approval of this resolution. 3. The Imperial Government's approval of this resolution will not affect in any way the right to take all necessary measures when it is deemed necessary to protect important and urgent interests in times of emergency. Bank of Japan Reduces Interest Rates 34

The trend towards lower interest rates is becoming increasingly apparent in Tokyo. As a result of consultations between the heads of eastern and western banks, it has been internally decided to reduce deposit interest rates starting from July 1st. This afternoon, the Deposit Agreement Executive Committee was held at the Bankers Association in Tokyo and Osaka. On the 29th, a general meeting of member banks of the Deposit Interest Association will be held to formally decide on the reduction of interest rates. The extent of the reduction will be 1.5% for both types A and B, 0.1% per diem for daily interest deposits, and current deposits will remain unchanged. (28th Dispatch from Dentsu)

The opportunity to reduce deposit interest rates at banks in Tokyo has arisen this year. At one time, due to the state of the economy, the situation for reducing interest rates was quite urgent. However, due to disagreements between eastern and western banks, it could not be realized. Recently, the opinions of eastern and western banks on this matter have gradually converged. On the 28th, the situation suddenly changed, and a committee was held at the Marunouchi Bankers' Association, deciding to convene a general meeting on the 29th to approve the reduction of deposit interest rates, which will be implemented from July 1st. (28th Dispatch from Japan United Press)

The banks in Tokyo held an emergency executive meeting on the afternoon of the 28th, where Mr. Ikeda, representing Mitsui Bank, proposed a reduction in deposit interest rates. As a result, it was decided to implement the interest rate reduction from July 1st, which will be submitted to the Bankers' Association for deliberation on the 29th. (28th Dispatch from Japan United Press)

The banks in Osaka also held an emergency meeting today and decided to reduce deposit interest rates. (28th Dispatch from Japan United Press)

Due to the decision of the banks to reduce deposit interest rates, the financial world will enter an era of low interest rates, and the Bank of Japan will also have to reduce interest rates. (28th Dispatch from Japan United Press)

Liu Guitang Sends a Telegram Announcing His Allegiance 50

Liu Guitang telegraphed from Beijing on the 26th, stating: "To all newspapers and organizations: Since the fall of Tokyo, the state affairs have become increasingly urgent. All members of the Chinese nation share a common hatred of the enemy. Guitang, a mere warrior, was compelled by righteousness to lead his troops out of the pass last year, vowing to resist Japan to the death, with the determination to save the country or perish with it. Embracing the firm will to live or die together, sinking our boats and breaking our pots, we wielded our weapons to kill the enemy, our blood splattered on the frontier grass, and we went deep into western Liaoning, displaying a spirit of sacrifice and repeatedly frustrating the enemy's arrogance. We could have advanced eastward with our victories and cleared the border areas, but the national army retreated, and we were isolated. We faced a strong enemy without and lacked food and ammunition within. However, we still raised our arms and called upon the starving soldiers to resist the elite troops, one against ten, supporting ourselves for several days without losing an inch of land. But heaven did not favor us, and the snow submerged our shins. Without clothing or food, the soldiers were freezing and starving to death, and their numbers were about to be halved. At this time, I originally wanted to sacrifice myself for the country and fulfill my national obligations, but I was afraid that sacrificing myself would not help the current difficulties. How about enduring humiliation and borrowing strength to seek future opportunities? My sincerity can be attested by heaven and earth. From then on, although environmental pressures have increased, my determination to kill the enemy has become firmer. I have been biding my time, not forgetting the shame of Kuaiji. Fortunately, I am now standing on the same front as the anti-Japanese allied forces, sharpening my weapons and preparing my horses, with my banners pointing east. I would rather be a hero in battle than a survivor under occupation. As we march to the border, our grief is overwhelming. We will eliminate this enemy before our morning meal and restore our mountains and rivers. As I send this telegram, my thoughts race, awaiting your instructions. Liu Guitang, August 28th, dispatch not completed." (28th Special Dispatch)

The government is currently considering confiscating the party's property, and it is widely believed that the government will soon seek an excuse to dissolve the Central Catholic Church.

All members of the National Sovereignty Party who have been arrested will be released, and all members of the National Sovereignty Party in the Prussian Parliament and the German Parliament will act in unison with the members of the National Socialist Party.

▲Reuters Berlin, 27th: The National Socialist government issued a declaration today stating that Jewish workers are not allowed to join trade unions, but Jewish people may organize their own Jewish trade unions, which will not be affiliated with German organizations. From now on, Jewish people may not join any German organizations.

Sensational Japanese Assassination Case Opens: Blood Pledge Corps' Conspiracy to Assassinate Key Figures 65

The Uprising Was Carried Out After the End of the Shanghai Incident

To Eliminate the Elder Statesmen and Overthrow the Privileged Class

▲Japan United Press, Tokyo, 28th: The first public trial of the Blood Pledge Corps' conspiracy to assassinate Mr. Junnosuke Inoue and Mr. Takuma Dan, and to attempt to assassinate prominent figures, opened at the Tokyo District Court at 9:00 AM on the 28th. The case has caused a sensation, and the details of the case are quite serious. Therefore, the audience flocked to the court last night to wait for the opening of the trial, but the authorities only allowed 62 of them to attend. After the judge, prosecutors, more than 20 defendants and their lawyers took their seats, the judge announced the opening of the trial. First, the identity of the defendant was investigated, and then the prosecutor stated the facts of the indictment.

▲Japan United Press, Tokyo, 28th: After the prosecutor finished stating the facts, the judge questioned the defendant Nissho Inoue on the following main issues:

Judge: "Is it true that the naval comrades decided to start an uprising after the Shanghai Incident was over?"

Inoue replied: "No, but they thought it would be better to decide to implement this matter separately."

Judge: "What was the method of assassination?"

Inoue replied: "It was originally planned to assassinate 20 representatives of the ruling class, but this was very difficult, so it was decided that each person would be responsible for killing one person."

Judge: "Is the defendant the ringleader?"

Inoue replied: "I was in charge of liaison and small-scale control affairs."

Judge: "Did you give special orders to the three defendants, Sho, Numahisago, and Kurosawa?"

Inoue replied: "I ordered them to be careful in carrying out their assigned goals." The judge and the defendant Inoue's answers lasted for more than two hours. At 11:50 AM, the court took a temporary recess and reopened at 1:00 PM to continue questioning Nissho Inoue.

Judge: "What kind of society does the defendant hope to realize and by what method?"

Inoue replied: "The method of building society has not been given much consideration, but I believe that Japanese party politics is the politics of a privileged class that despises the constitution. To break the current situation of Japan's impasse, it is necessary to first reform party politics, and to eliminate the elder statesmen and ask for the Emperor's judgment, so that the privileged class and the tyrannical can be punished for the crimes of the political parties."

Judge: "What are your thoughts now about your plan to assassinate?"

Inoue replied: "I have no special thoughts, but I am certain about the reasons for establishing this plan. I am prepared to die, but it is necessary to reform the current society."

Judge: "Did the defendant know that the assassination plan violated the law?" Inoue: "I knew it. I originally wanted to act legally, but because the current situation is an emergency, I am determined to break the law in an emergency to reform society. I am now awaiting death, please give me a fair trial."

The court adjourned at 2:35 PM. The second public trial will open at 9:00 AM on the 30th.

Military Disarmament Meeting Adjourns Until October 66

▲Reuters, Geneva, 27th - The main committee of the Disarmament Conference today decided to postpone the meeting until October 16th. However, this decision still needs to be approved by the General Committee on Thursday. The main committee will meet in September to listen to the results of Henderson's talks with the major powers and prepare the second reading draft of the British disarmament plan. This postponement to autumn is the result of an agreement reached yesterday between Henderson and Paul-Boncour in Paris. At the same time, Henderson expressed his opinion that negotiations between individual representatives should be conducted during the break from now until the resumption of the meeting.

▲Havas, Geneva, 27th - The Presidium of the Disarmament Conference met at 3:30 PM, chaired by Henderson. Despite the opposition of the German representative Nadolny, the Presidium decided to recommend to the General Committee, which will meet on Thursday, that the Disarmament Conference be postponed until October 16th.

▲Havas, Geneva, 27th - The Presidium of the Disarmament Conference met for only half an hour. Chairman Henderson advocated a temporary postponement of the meeting, waiting until his negotiations could achieve the necessary compromises before reconvening. The British representative Eden and the French representative Massigli both agreed. The Italian and Soviet delegations did not participate in the discussion. It was then decided to convene the General Committee on Thursday for a final decision. It is generally believed that the General Committee will approve the proposal for postponement when it meets on Thursday.

The Strength of the Luan River (Luanxi) Puppet Army Increases Daily 70

=Military Content is Generally Northern Soldiers Transportation of Vehicles and Recovery of Ash=

Special dispatch from Peiping (Beiping). There is still no definite solution for the puppet army led by Li Jichun in the Luan River area. North China is in danger. Rectifying the situation is extremely difficult. The details of the puppet army's disturbances and its organizational overview are recorded below. The seriousness of the Luan River problem existed before the armistice agreement was signed.

Overview of the Puppet Army's Organization 71

The puppet army led by Li Jichun and others took advantage of the Japanese army's disturbances in North China to occupy the area east and west of the Luan River, with ambitious intentions. Our army, due to many concerns, was restrained. Suppression was unsuccessful, and appeasement was not easy. Hesitation led to the puppet army's growing strength, making a solution more difficult. Now it has become a serious problem. The root cause is that domestic wars have been frequent in the past, and the political situation has not been stable, which has led past warlords and politicians to be lured by Japanese interests to go to the Northeast and act as accomplices under Japanese control, willingly betraying their country. Since the September 18th Incident, illegal organizations in Changchun have been established one after another. Many soldiers from the Zhili-Lu (Zhilu) faction have secretly left for Manchuria to join the puppet state. The Japanese then ordered them to form their own armies, directly subordinate to the puppet state and indirectly controlled and commanded by the Japanese, implementing a policy of "using Chinese to control Chinese." Five armies were established one after another: (1) the First Army of Pacifying the Country, (2) the Second Army of Building the Country, (3) the Third Army of Protecting the Country, (4) the Fourth Army of Stabilizing the Country, and (5) the Fifth Army of Defending the Country. The First Army of Pacifying the Country was Yu Zhishan's unit, the Second Army of Building the Country was Cheng Guorui's unit, the Third Army of Protecting the Country was Huang Xiling's unit, the Fourth Army of Stabilizing the Country was Liu Peichen's unit, and the Fifth Army of Defending the Country was Zhao Huiqing's unit. Each recruited soldiers and horses and set up their own banners. Their troops were mostly composed of old Zhili-Lu soldiers and bandits from outside the pass. They were generally trained for three months and then formally formed into armies by order of the puppet military and political departments. Guns and ammunition were partly supplied by the Japanese, and the army's salaries were mostly raised locally. Although there were many people, the command was extremely uncoordinated, and there were often internal conflicts. The organization was disorganized. The Japanese were only using them temporarily. The greatest purpose was to make "Chinese kill Chinese." Initially, Yu Zhishan was the commander of the First Army of Pacifying the Country. Cheng Guorui gathered his old troops and led them to Changchun, where he was appointed by the Japanese as the commander of the Second Army of Building the Country of Manchuria, with Cheng as the commander-in-chief, directly commanding the army, claiming to have twenty regiments. Fang Yongchang was appointed as the chief of staff, and Liu Peichen was appointed as the deputy commander. Fang was expelled shortly after due to opposition from his subordinates. Liu also disagreed with Cheng and competed for military power, secretly fighting each other. Because Liu's strength was weak, he eventually lost and resigned from his position as puppet deputy commander. He formed another army, which was the Fourth Army, and appointed Jin Bihui as the deputy commander. Jin was the daughter of Prince Su of the former Qing dynasty. She had been in Japan for a long time and was also known as Kawashima Yoshiko. She had once gone to Manchuria with her brother Jin Bidong to persuade Su Bingwen. She was very beautiful and had an ambiguous relationship with Tada, a Japanese senior advisor to the puppet state, and thus obtained this position. At that time, scandalous secrets spread throughout the puppet capital. However, the army was disbanded only half a month after its formation because there were too few soldiers and more officers than soldiers. A unit of Cheng Guorui's puppet army also mutinied, so he resigned. The vacancy of commander of the Second Puppet Army was filled by Huang Xiling. The Fifth Army of Zhao Huiqing was also eliminated by the Japanese. At that time, the Rehe (Jehol) incident occurred. Zhao led his puppet army to western Liaoning in March of this year. When they arrived at Xinlitun, they suddenly encountered more than 50 members of the Japanese garrison on the way. The Japanese army mistakenly thought they were our volunteer army and prepared to encircle and attack them. Zhao was also furious and killed all the Japanese commanders and advisors in the army, leaving their bodies in front of the battle. The Japanese army then swept them with machine guns. Zhao also surrounded all the Japanese soldiers. None of the 50 survived. In this battle, they also captured ten machine guns. Just as they were preparing to revolt, the Japanese found out and sent a large unit to eliminate Zhao's troops. Zhao and his subordinate officers were all shot. The Fifth Army disintegrated without a trace. When the war in eastern Luanhe (Luandong) broke out, Li Jichun, due to his relationship with the first Tianjin Incident, requested the Kwantung Army to be the vanguard. If they could capture Tianjin and Peiping, they would give him the Luanhe area as a reward. At first, there were only a little over a thousand people. Later, Zhao Lei and others defected, and he recruited bandits everywhere, creating the current situation. In addition, Hao Peng, Bai Jianwu, and others united with Li. The plainclothes team that recently rioted in Tianjin was transported to Qinhuangdao to be commanded by Li. His power became even more rampant.

The People of Luanxi Are in Dire Straits 72

The puppet army led by Li Jichun and Zhao Lei and others, under the name of the puppet National Salvation Army, occupy the area around the Luan River and the railway line. Shi Yousan is still in Qinhuangdao, plotting activities. Li's puppet headquarters is located inside Tangshan Jiaotong University. Li himself is also in Tangshan. The area from Tianzhuang to Xugezhuang on the Beining Railway is garrisoned by Li's troops. When the Japanese army withdraws from one place, he follows up and fills the position. Food and salaries are also becoming increasingly sufficient. Taxes are levied arbitrarily, and the people are in dire straits. The strength has increased rapidly, making it difficult to resolve. Our side previously contacted the Japanese embassy, hoping to implement the truce agreement. The Japanese embassy's military attache, Nagatsu, took our side's opinions to Changchun to meet with the Kwantung Army Commander Muto for consultation. There has been no reply for a long time. Negotiations with the Japanese embassy's secretary, Nakayama, are continuing in the hope that the puppet army issue can be resolved quickly. It is rumored in Beijing that the puppet army will withdraw 20 li from the railway line, but this has not yet been implemented. The Japanese and puppet troops in Lugou still guard the railway and harass us from time to time. At about 10 p.m. on the 26th, the puppet army from the village fired at us, but we did not retaliate. The situation was quickly calmed down. There are still more than 200 puppet troops stationed in Ninghe City. After Nagatsu went to Changchun, he was suddenly dispatched by the Japanese General Staff to leave China for inspections in various countries for a period of two years. Nagatsu has now rushed to Harbin from Changchun, and it is said that he may not return to Peiping for the time being. His position as a military attache at the Japanese embassy will be concurrently held by Shibayama. Shibayama has now arrived in Shanghai and will soon leave Shanghai for the north. In the future, our side will continue to negotiate with Shibayama on the disposal of the puppet army, and it is difficult to reach a concrete solution at this time.

Beining (Peiping-Mukden) Railway Eastern Line Through Traffic Issue 73

Qian Zongze, the director of the Beining Railway Bureau, came to Peiping to meet with He Yingqin and Huang Fu to discuss the issue of the Beining Railway's through traffic with the Japanese side. He returned to Tianjin yesterday to continue negotiations. At noon today, Qian Fu arrived in Peiping from Tianjin and visited the military and political authorities to report on everything. According to Qian, the issue of through traffic is in progress and will be realized in the near future, but there is no concrete decision yet. The eastbound train only reaches Lutai. The Beining Railway's income has sharply decreased since the route was shortened. Although the Sino-Japanese truce agreement was signed long ago, the puppet army in Luanxi is still disturbing the railway line, causing many obstacles. Various countries have criticized this. The issue of through traffic is a matter of urgency. The international train that arrived in Lutai from Tianjin the other day, after repeated negotiations with the puppet army by the Americans, the puppet army only allowed it to open to Tangshan. If it goes east, there are many bandits along the way and they cannot be responsible. Therefore, the Americans did not dare to try it easily and returned to Tianjin. In short, unless the puppet army is transferred away, the issue of through traffic cannot be resolved. It is rumored that the Beining Railway plans to conduct a trial run of international trains to Qinhuangdao on July 1. Huang Fu and He Yingqin have agreed to contact the Japanese side, but it is not yet known whether it can be realized. The railway is in economic straits and will implement large-scale layoffs in the coming days to avoid owing salaries. There are many idle employees at the various stations of the railway bureau, and without doing so, it is not enough to balance income and expenditure. Qian returned to Tianjin by car this afternoon after completing his official duties to plan everything. (June 27)

The Central Government Does Not Advocate the Use of Force in Chahar 74

The Chahar Affair is Still the Responsibility of the Government Directly

Kong Xiangxi Will Visit Yan Xishan in Hebian

Special dispatch from Peiping. Feng Yuxiang's attitude of advocating resistance against Japan and protecting Chahar has remained unchanged. The Zhangjiakou incident, due to Song Zheyuan's mediation, has sent representatives several times to negotiate with Feng, and there has been hope for a peaceful resolution for a time. Recently, Song Zheyuan was ordered to return to Chahar, and someone is responsible for the Chahar provincial administration. The central government has also agreed to properly resettle the various armies of Fang Zhenwu and Deng Wen, which is progressing smoothly. Suddenly, there was another twist. Zhang Jiyong went to Zhangjiakou again, but to no avail. After returning to Peiping on the 23rd, he submitted Feng's four proposed opinions to Song and forwarded them to He Yingqin and Huang Fu for detailed discussion. Everyone felt that the Chahar affair was difficult. That night, they telegraphed the central government and Commander Chiang Kai-shek for instructions. So far, no reply telegram has arrived in Peiping. The various parties believe that the issue of the puppet army in Luanxi has not been resolved for a long time, and the Japanese side's opinions on the truce agreement are quite inconsistent internally. The withdrawal of the Japanese army is still extremely slow. If the situation in eastern Chahar changes, the overall situation in North China will be affected, and the future crisis is unimaginable. Therefore, they are quite anxious about Feng's recent attitude. Now Song Zheyuan has expressed that he will not return to Chahar for the time being. The first step in the authorities' decision on the Chahar affair is still to seek a solution by peaceful means. They do not want to lightly start a war. Even if it is unavoidable, they will not use force internally. All measures are carefully handled with the aim of consolidating the security of Chahar Province and ensuring that North China, which has been turned from danger to safety, is not affected by the Chahar affair. As for how to protect Chahar Province, they have always advocated that the government should be directly responsible. For example, the puppet armies of Liu Guitang, Cui Xingwu, and others in eastern Chahar have long been under the protection of the Japanese. Their organizations are not sound, and their intentions are unpredictable. In order to eliminate the rebels, it is impossible to tolerate them. How to deal with them in the future is still under consideration.

The central government has now decided to send Kong Xiangxi north to inspect and visit Yan Xishan in Bingyi on the way. Yan Xishan has now returned to his hometown of Hebian Village for a short rest. Kong will take a plane from Shanghai to Peiping on the 27th and will go directly to Hebian to meet with Yan to convey the central government's intentions. Yan's recent attitude has been consistent with the central government. Although he has not expressed anything to Feng, in addition to protecting Shanxi and developing industry, he will probably not participate in this anti-Japanese military action in Chahar. (June 25)

Liu Guitang Defects 75

Liu Has Led His Troops to Retreat to Guyuan

Kangbao and Baochang Have Both Been Recovered

Fang Ji and Other Troops Concentrated in Zhangbei

Special dispatch from Peiping. After Zhangjiakou decided to send troops to resist Japan and recover the lost territory, Feng Yuxiang appointed Fang Zhenwu as the commander of the Northern Route Army, Ji Hongchang as the commander of the Northern Route Army, Deng Wen as the left deputy commander, and Li Zhongyi as the right deputy commander. After receiving the order, Fang and others telegraphed their appointments. Their troops were concentrated in Zhangbei and advanced on separate routes. Liu Guitang also telegraphed his defection, and his troops retreated to Guyuan, preparing to counterattack western Rehe. Liu's telegram also stated his loyalty to the enemy. The original telegram is as follows: "Since the fall of the Northeast, I have served the Japanese, and all of my Chinese nation hate the enemy. Guitang, a soldier, is obliged to resist Japan. Last year, I led my troops out of the pass and fought to the death against Japan, determined to survive or die with the territory, and determined to die with the land. I smashed the pot and broke the boat, and I killed the enemy with my spears. Blood splattered on the border grass, and I went deep into western Liaoning. With the spirit of sacrifice, I repeatedly frustrated the enemy's power. I could have taken advantage of the victory to advance eastward and pacify the border. However, the national army retreated westward, and I was isolated. There was an enemy outside, and there was no food or ammunition inside. However, I still shouted and drove the hungry soldiers to resist the elite troops, fighting with injuries, fighting one against ten, and supporting for several months without losing an inch of land. But heaven did not help me. The snow fell to my knees, and there was no clothing or food. The soldiers died of hunger and cold, and nearly half of them died. At this time, I wanted to die for my country and fulfill my obligations as a citizen. But I was afraid that killing myself would not help the situation. How could I endure humiliation and burden, and gradually claim to be a state, borrowing capital to take advantage, and the blood can be tested by heaven and sun? From then on, the environment pressed, and I increased my wisdom in judging the enemy, and I tasted the shame of Kuaiji, and I could not forget it. Then I was fortunate to stand on the same front with my anti-Japanese friendly army, feeding the horses and encouraging the soldiers, and the flag pointed to the east. I would rather be a hero in the battlefield than a coward in peacetime. Revitalize the frontier. I cannot bear the grief and indignation. Destroy this dynasty and eat, return my mountains and rivers, and face the gods. I hope that Liu Gui is forgiven."

Fang and Shi ancient style [unclear characters], Ji immediately set up a command headquarters in Zhangbei, commanding the various troops to advance eastward. Deng Wen, Li Zhong [unclear character] · Nie Yuling · the various armies and Wang Shiming and other [unclear character] detachments also gradually concentrated in Zhangbei and moved out on separate routes. Zhang Renjie's division of Fang's troops also sent a part to Zhangbei. Before Feng took office, Liu Guitang sent personnel to contact him to surrender. Recently, he sent his deputy commander Shang Wu as a representative to be responsible for discussing surrender and anti-Japanese methods with Feng. Feng held the tenet that those who resist Japan are friends, and Liu became resolute in the defection. His troops stationed in Kangbao and Baochang began to withdraw to Guyuan on the 22nd. Most of them have now concentrated in Guyuan. Kangbao and Baochang were recovered on the 24th and garrisoned by Wang Shiming's detachment. Today (27th), Feng has sent a telegram to Peiping, reporting that Kangbao and Baochang have been recovered and is currently advancing towards Doron. In addition to a unit of Japanese troops, Moki Cavalry, stationed in the Doron area, there are also more than 2,000 rebel troops under Cui Xingwang. Cui has also sent personnel to contact Feng to surrender. Now the Northern Route Anti-Japanese Army is preparing to contact Liu Guitang's troops after most of them are concentrated in Kangbao and Baochang, and then attack Doron, hoping to completely recover the lost territory in eastern Chahar in the shortest period of time. (June 27)

Anti-Shen (Honglie) Movement in the Northeast Navy 76

Shen's Attitude is Passive and Has Telegraphed to the Central Government to Resign

The Haiqi and Other Three Ships Freely Sail Out of the Port

Qingdao Communication. Shen Honglie, the commander of the Northeast Navy and the mayor of Qingdao, was unsuccessfully assassinated by his subordinate Feng Zhichong at the Dagang pier at 4 p.m. on the 24th of this month, as reported in the previous newspaper. Because the matter is important, the reporter inquired from all parties and personally visited Mr. Shen to inquire about everything. The information obtained is recorded as follows:

▲Reasons for the Assassination There are two reasons for this incident: (1) Since Mr. Shen also held the position of mayor, the lower-level officers of the Northeast Navy, which he directly controlled, believed that the opportunity to get promoted and make a fortune had arrived. Therefore, they all wanted to seize a seat as the chief of the Qingdao Municipal Public Security Bureau, the captain of the security team, and the important officials of the various agencies under the municipal government. However, Mr. Shen has never changed a single important official of the various agencies under the municipal government unless there are special circumstances. His subordinates were inevitably disappointed with Mr. Shen because their desires were not fulfilled. This is the first reason for resentment among subordinates. (2) Mr. Shen has recently been very serious about the ban on smoking. A few months ago, Mr. Shen instructed the officials of both the municipal government and the navy that anyone addicted to this habit must quit within a time limit. If they do not quit after the deadline, they will be dismissed once discovered. Even close relatives will not be lightly spared. Many lower-level officers of the navy are addicted to these bad habits. Although Mr. Shen has repeatedly ordered and emphasized it, many of those who complied with the deadline to quit are indeed few, and those who ignore the command are also numerous. Therefore, several people have been investigated by Mr. Shen and given the punishment of dismissal, and those who have not been investigated are also uneasy. This is the second reason for resentment among subordinates. In addition, the Northeast Navy originally owed military pay for as long as four months. After Mr. Shen also became the mayor, his subordinates hoped that Mr. Shen would use the income from Qingdao to pay off the arrears. However, after Mr. Shen took office as mayor, he did not create a source of income for the navy. Old arrears were not mentioned. This is also one of the reasons for resentment among subordinates.

▲Details of the Assassination Since Mr. Shen had caused resentment among his subordinates, the lower-level officers of the navy had a brewing anti-Shen movement (but the interior was not unanimous, and there were also those who advocated supporting Shen). Feng Zhichong, the gunner of the Zhenhai ship, was one of the anti-Shen members. At 4 p.m. on the 24th of this month, when Shen took the Haiwang small launch from the Dagang wharf to the Zhenhai ship for a speech, Feng also went on the same boat, in addition to Shen's follower Shi Fusheng (Shen usually did not have guards when he went out, only taking a servant). When the boat left the wharf and sailed not far, Feng took out a pistol from his side and shot at Shen, firing three shots in a row, all of which missed. Fortunately, Shen's follower Shi Fusheng was beside him and rushed forward to push Feng away. Feng fell into the water. At that time, Shen remained calm and composed, and was escorted by Shi to the Zhenhai ship for a speech to the officers and soldiers. Shi then returned by small launch. At that time, Feng had been fished up with cedar planks by the Dagang branch of the Third Public Security Bureau. Shi explained the situation of Feng's assassination, and a Browning pistol and 89 bullets were found on Feng's body. Since the pistol he had previously held had fallen into the sea, Feng was guarded by the branch. After being interrogated by the naval headquarters in the evening, he was executed by shooting the next morning.

▲Jointly Overthrowing Shen After this incident, Mr. Shen originally did not want to pursue the matter too much, so he only had Feng shot dead. Unexpectedly, Feng's accomplices and others, because Shen quickly imposed a heavy punishment on Feng, jointly launched a movement to overthrow Shen with other lower-level officers. Among them, the pro-Shen faction was isolated and weak and was coerced by the crowd and dared not resist. The party also falsely used the name of the entire navy to demand that Mr. Shen step down. Important officials of the naval headquarters and the captains of the various ships stationed in Qingdao have been gathering in the headquarters for days to discuss solutions. While the matter was being discussed, the Haiqi, Haichen, and Zhaoe three ships berthed in the rear actually disobeyed the orders of their superiors (the captains of the three ships were not on the ships) and took free action on the 26th, sailing out of the port (some say they went south, some say they went to Weihai, not knowing which is true). And this matter has become increasingly stiff and cannot be resolved. However, it is heard that Mr. Shen's personal attitude has been extremely negative since suffering this blow. He is eager to take this opportunity to step back and recuperate. It is heard that yesterday he telegraphed to the Central Military Commission and the Executive Yuan, requesting to resign from his positions as naval commander and Qingdao mayor. It is not yet known whether he will be approved.

▲Shen's Talk According to Shen's talk to the reporter, I have asked myself that I have always been upright in my life and dealings with people. Unfortunately, this change happened, which is beyond my expectation. But I will never be discouraged because of this. Before the central government approves my resignation, I will do my duty for one day in office and will never give up my post. (June 27)

The Opening Ceremony of the Sujia Highway Was Held 77

=The Total Length is 76 Kilometers and the Construction Cost is More Than 700,000 Yuan=

The Sujia Highway is one of the six major highways set by the National Economic Commission. Yesterday (28th) at 10:00 a.m., the opening ceremony was held at the Suzhou Mudu Bridge. Important officials from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces attended the ceremony. Zeng Yangfu, the Director of the Construction Department of Zhejiang Province, and Dong Xiujia, the Director of the Construction Department of Jiangsu Province, both gave earnest speeches. At around 11:00 a.m., Madam Qin Fen cut the line to open the road, and the guests took the car directly to Jiaxing. After arriving in Jiaxing, the Zhejiang Provincial Government hosted a lunch at the Yanyu Tower. The details are recorded below:

Meeting Situation 78

Yesterday at 10 AM, Zhejiang Construction Bureau Chief Zeng Yangfu, Jiangsu Construction Bureau Chief Dong Xiujia, National Economic Council Member Qin Fen, Finance Ministry Secretary Guo Dehua, accompanied by his wife Guo Huang Qianhong, and Wuxian Construction Bureau Technician Qian Tianpeng, arrived at the venue one after another. A wooden stage was temporarily erected at the venue, with a white cloth banner inscribed with the seven characters "Suzhou-Jiaxing Road Opening Ceremony." A flower basket, a gift from the Ford Motor Company, was placed on the stage. American Commercial Counselor Smith, Shanghai Municipal Council Political Department Representative Shaweness, and Shanghai Municipal Council Merchant Corps Commander Thomas also went early to attend. The meeting began at 10 AM. First, Zhejiang Construction Bureau Chief Zeng Yangfu delivered a speech, roughly stating that he was representing the Zhejiang Provincial Government today to attend the opening ceremony. He noted that the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road is crucial for connecting the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Although there were difficulties during construction, it was ultimately completed due to the joint efforts of the two provincial governments. In the past year, the completed highways in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces include the Nanjing-Hangzhou Road, Nanjing-Wuhu Road, and Xuan-Chang Road, and the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road is also completed and opened to traffic today. However, the road surface of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road cannot be compared with urban roads due to various reasons. Each kilometer of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road costs only six to seven thousand yuan, which is five to six times less than the value of urban roads in Shanghai. However, this road is designed for transportation, not for aesthetics like urban roads. Therefore, we must look at it from a different perspective. Next, Jiangsu Construction Bureau Chief Dong Xiujia delivered a speech, roughly saying, "The Suzhou-Jiaxing Road was completed in a short period, and the National Economic Council has made a great contribution. If the council had not provided economic and technical assistance, the completion of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road would likely have been delayed for several months. After the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road is opened to traffic, the transportation between Suzhou and Jiaxing can avoid the trouble of detouring through Shanghai, saving time and money, and boosting the financial flow between Jiangsu and Zhejiang. However, as the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road passes through a corner of Taihu Lake, some people may suspect that the bandits in Taihu Lake may have malicious plans. However, the reason for the rampant bandits in Taihu Lake is actually due to inconvenient transportation. Now that transportation is convenient, the bandits in Taihu Lake will naturally not dare to plot anything again, and the military and police's suppression of bandits will also be greatly effective due to the completion of this road. The Jiangsu Construction Bureau is currently planning to build a Suzhou ring road to revitalize the Suzhou business market," and so on. Following this, Qin Fen reported on the construction of the road. It was already 11 AM when the bell rang, and Qin Fen's wife then performed the ribbon-cutting ceremony. Secretary Zhu of the National Economic Council presented a silver scissors, over a foot long, to Mrs. Qin. Mrs. Qin held the scissors and cut the red ribbon placed across the road. At that moment, applause erupted, cheering "Long live the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road!" Six cars, full of guests, slowly drove onto the road. A cargo truck, carrying a team of the Wuxian Security Corps, led the way with armed protection. The other cars followed in a single file. A car belonging to Zhejiang Construction Bureau Chief Zeng Yangfu and a charcoal-powered car followed behind. After leaving the meeting venue at Mudu Bridge, the first major bridge encountered was the newly built Xindai Bridge. After ten minutes, the cars crossed the bridge. At 12 PM, they arrived in Wujiang, Suzhou; at 12:25 PM, they arrived in Beishe; at 12:50 PM, they passed Pingwang; at 1:10 PM, they passed Shengze; at 1:45 PM, they passed Wangjiangjing. Due to the uneven road surface along the way, the cars could not drive quickly. At 2:30 PM, they finally arrived in Jiaxing. The Zhejiang Provincial Government specially prepared lunch at the Nanhu Misty Rain Tower, inviting the special guests to cross the lake. The Jiaxing watercrafts... continued the protection... afterward, the guests... the cars... still... cars... situation... below,

Transportation Relationship 79

Jiaxing... Remaining... Committee... Liu Suzhou-Zhejiang-Anhui three provinces' contact highway, and again for the seven provinces' connecting public from Jiang... The Suzhou Road Changshu Zhapu branch line is one segment, starting in Zhou, passing through Wujiang, Bachichi, Pingwang, Shengze, Wangjiangjing to... Jiaxing, a total length of 66. kilometers, is the main road connecting the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou... roads, and is a shortcut for transportation between Suzhou and Jia... Furthermore, this association and the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provincial governments are currently preparing... at both ends of this road,... Zhapu to Jiaxing, Suzhou to Wuxi, Shanghai to Suzhou, etc.,... circulating and connecting, its convenience is even more... However, this road is located in a water area, with particularly many bridges and culverts,... repeatedly surveyed, to connect important cities, not hesitating to repeatedly change the route. Between winter and spring, rain and snow are continuous, and construction is often hindered. Counting from the beginning of construction to completion,... time has passed over a year, the more difficult the beginning, the greater the joy of success. Looking back on the past, it is worth pondering.

Construction Process 80

The area traversed by the road is under the jurisdiction of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, so the construction was undertaken separately by the construction departments of the two provinces. Planning began in June of the 21st year of the Republic of China, and the entire road was completed in June of this year, taking exactly one year from start to finish. The construction process of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang sections is described separately as follows: (1) Jiangsu Section: This section starts from the customs house east of Panmen in Suzhou and ends at Wangjiangjing Town on the Jiangsu-Zhejiang border, with a total length of 52.1 kilometers. The northern section of the roadbed was started in the 19th year of the Republic of China. The Suzhou to Wujiang section was built by requisitioned labor by the Wuxian Construction Bureau, but the width was only 5 meters. The Wujiang to Bachichi section was also once built by requisitioned labor by the Wujiang County Construction Bureau, but the roadbed was only in its rudimentary form, with a significant difference in height. Bridge and culvert projects were also undertaken by the construction bureaus of the two counties. A total of ten reinforced concrete bridges, ten wooden bridges, five culverts, and more than eighty water pipes were completed in the Suzhou-Wujiang section. The route south of Bachichi passes through numerous rivers, with a low-lying terrain, and the engineering was quite extensive. The counties were limited by financial resources, so construction had been delayed for a long time. In May of the 21st year of the Republic of China, the council recognized that the road was extremely important for transportation between the two provinces and should be completed quickly. Therefore, the road was listed as one of the three provinces' connecting highways, and Guo Lian consultant Ao Jingji was assigned to jointly survey the Pinghu to Wangjiangjing section of the route with the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department. The original route of this section was to pass through the Grand Canal from Bachichi, along the east bank to Pingwang Town, then cross the river and head straight to Wangjiangjing. It required the construction of two large bridges, and the villages and towns passed through were also more remote. Consultant Ao suggested changing the route, going along the west bank of the Grand Canal from Bachichi, passing west of Pingwang Town, passing Shengze Town, and heading to areas that could be expected to develop. The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department followed his advice and ordered the county to remeasure. Once the route was determined, the Suwang Section Engineering Office was established in Pingwang in August of the same year. After September, various projects were started one after another. By the end of the 21st year of the Republic of China, 70-80% of the roadbed earthwork and bridge projects had been completed, and a large amount of road surface materials had also been transported. However, due to the continuous rain and snow in winter, the progress of the project was slower in January and February of the 22nd year. After March, it resumed active progress, and the bridge, culvert, embankment, retaining wall, and road surface projects were completed successively. (2) Zhejiang Section: This section starts from the Grand Canal Bridge outside Jiaxing City and ends at Wangjiangjing on the Jiangsu-Zhejiang border, with a total length of 14.7 kilometers. After the council included this section in the three provinces' connecting highways in May of the 21st year of the Republic of China, the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau planned and implemented the project, establishing the Jiawang Section Engineering Office in Jiaxing. The entire section started construction simultaneously. Because the mileage was short and the area was a plain, construction was relatively easy, so the project progressed very quickly. The entire section of roadbed earthwork was completed in October of the 21st year of the Republic of China, and the bridge, culvert, and water pipe projects were also completed in November of the same year. However, the Grand Canal Bridge near Jiaxing was a larger project and was not completed until April of this year. The road surface project was completed in early March of this year.

Project Overview 81

The entire Suzhou-Jiaxing Road project was carried out in accordance with the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provincial Highway Engineering Standards and the highway engineering standards stipulated by the council. Because the entire road route passes through plains, the grades and curves are quite good. Only the grades near the bridgeheads are slightly steeper, but still not more than 3%. The radius of curvature is more than 70 meters. The load-bearing capacity of the bridges is 12 tons in the Suzhou-Jiaxing section, and slightly less in the Zhejiang section. A sectional description of the project overview is given below: (1) Jiangsu Section: The roadbed width is 7.5 meters. In addition to the approximately 100,000 cubic meters of earthwork already completed by the county government, approximately 480,000 cubic meters of new earthwork was done. The width of the crushed brick soil surface in the middle is 2 meters. The bridgeheads and areas near the lakes were widened appropriately to facilitate passing vehicles. In addition to the bridges and culverts already built by the county construction bureau, 43 new wooden bridges were built, the largest of which was the Dai Bridge near Suzhou. The bridge was originally intended to utilize the existing stone arch bridge, but after the Jiangsu Construction Department sent personnel to investigate in detail, it was found that the width of the bridge was insufficient, and the bridge foundation and arch were gradually collapsing, which was not conducive to traffic. Even if it could be widened and reinforced, the result would likely still be unsuitable. Therefore, it was decided to build a new wooden bridge about 60 meters west of the old bridge, with a total of 29 spans, measuring 232 meters in length. The bridge deck line adopts an arched shape, so the middle spans are quite high above the water surface, allowing ships to pass through. The length of the other bridges varies from 6 meters to over 60 meters. In addition, there are ten reinforced concrete culverts and 157 concrete water pipes in the entire section. The route from Bachichi to Pingwang passes through the three lakes of Tangjia Lake, Majia Lake, and San Dang. The lake water is very deep, and it is difficult to obtain soil for filling, so the earthwork for filling is quite difficult. Because one side faces the river and the other side faces the lake, there is concern that the wind and waves will erode the roadbed and cause it to collapse. Stone retaining walls were built on both sides of the embankment, and stone slopes were built on the embankment slope, rising above the water surface for protection. The three lakes' retaining walls are over 1,500 meters long, costing over 57,000 yuan. The total project budget for the entire section, as approved by the council, is 562,920 yuan, with a road construction fund of 180,134 yuan borrowed from the council. (2) Zhejiang Section: The roadbed width is 7.5 meters. The total earthwork is approximately 135,000 cubic meters. The width of the road surface in the middle is 3 meters. The road surface material is crushed brick in the lower layer and crushed stone in the upper layer. This is because this section is closer to Ganpu, where mountain stone can be mined and transported, so crushed stone road surface is used as appropriate. There are a total of 18 bridges, of which the Grand Canal Bridge near Jiaxing is the largest project. The river is wide and the traffic is very frequent, so a reinforced concrete truss bridge was built to ensure its strength. The entire bridge has eight spans, with a total length of 76 meters. The remaining 17 bridges are all wooden bridges, ranging in length from 6 meters to 28 meters. The total project budget for the entire section, as approved by the council, is 141,443 yuan, with a road construction fund of 45,262 yuan borrowed from the council. In summary, the total project budget for the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road Jiangsu and Zhejiang sections, as approved by the council, is 704,363 yuan, of which the road construction fund borrowed from the council is 225,396 yuan. Among the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui connecting highways, this road project is the most significant, apart from the Hangzhou...

Roadside Facilities 82

This road... transportation... and... still have (1) cars, the Hangzhou Jiaxing long-distance bus, Jiangsu Province Construction... handle, this hall is organizing a long-distance bus... preparing various matters, currently transporting new cars... to Suzhou for use, scheduled to officially open for business on July 1st, (2) bus stations, in the Jiangsu section of this road, there are Suzhou, Wujiang, Bachichi, Pingwang, Shengze, five stations, currently being planned and charted by the Jiangsu section engineering office, in the Zhejiang section, there are three stations in Jiaxing Shuangqiao Wangjiangjing, each building a station, the Jiaxing station is also built with a four-bay garage, now completed, the mileage of each station is omitted, (3) road maintenance and long-distance telephone, the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road long-distance bus preparation office, in order to ensure the safety of passengers and the convenience of driving, plans to install long-distance telephones in each station to communicate information, as for the sanitation matters, in addition to the police protection of each county and town along the road, it is also planned to set up a road police team to be solely responsible for the security of the line,

Mr. Dong's Talk 83

Also, according to Jiangsu Construction Bureau Chief Dong Xiujia's discussion on the practical problems of various road surfaces, roughly, there are many types of road surfaces, but the choice depends on the amount of road construction funds and traffic conditions, and cannot be generalized. Speaking of its advantages and disadvantages, according to the current situation of insufficient government financial resources and rural economic bankruptcy in our country, it does not seem necessary to demand how beautiful it is, as long as the road surface can be consolidated. Therefore, the most suitable road bureau in our country at present, (1) rubble road, (2) crushed brick road, (3) crushed stone road, among the three, rubble road is the most suitable, because the rubble road is made of stone blocks, and no matter what skill is required during paving, anyone can engage in this work, which is most suitable for the system of requisitioning labor for road construction. Although its appearance is not very beautiful, it is quite durable in substance, and can last for a long time without breaking. The road maintenance work after the road is completed is relatively easy, and even if there is damage, one or two stone pieces can be replaced at any time without major repairs. A part of the Suzhou section of the Jingwu Road surface is made of rubble, and it has been nine months since then. After a recent inspection, it was found that the rubble has not changed. Based on this, its advantages can be proved. Crushed brick road is made of crushed brick, which is more solid than rubble road, but the price required is too high. The current section of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road is using this kind of road surface. Crushed stone road is made of crushed stone flattened. Although the road surface seems beautiful, it is extremely non-durable. Once the road surface is washed by wind and rain, it is very easy to damage, and the yellow mud and yellow sand mix together and float on the road surface, which is very easy to slip. After the car travels, the mud track peaks up, so the road maintenance project is very large at ordinary times. Although the construction cost is slightly saved, it is quite uneconomical in comparison. The Anhui section of the Jingwu Road is this kind of road surface. At first glance, it is very beautiful. However, the characteristic of these three kinds of road surfaces is that the cost is slightly cheaper, and so on. (Daily News)

Songjiang 84

A Strange Story of He Runzhang's Suicide

Hu Runzhang, a resident of Dawu Bridge in this city, has a moderately wealthy family and is quite self-sufficient. When the Hu Yinglong wife-killing case occurred in the past, Runzhang lived in a collateral branch of respected relatives and was repeatedly summoned by the court for questioning. Because Runzhang was solitary by nature, he was quite unhappy about this. The stimulation deepened day by day, and he gradually developed mental illness. Recently, he has been living at home behind closed doors, rarely contacting the outside world. He often felt厌... At times, behind everyone's back, he used the red-headed rope of the bedstead bamboo to tie around his neck in the room. His feet did not leave the ground, but he was tragically strangled to death. When his family discovered it, it was too late to save him. Those who spoke about it all expressed their astonishment.

Five Warehouse Township Villagers Robbed

At the home of Zhuang Hehe, a villager in Wu Warehouse Township, on the night of the 26th, suddenly eight or nine bandits speaking a local dialect broke into the house, dragged the victim from the bed, tied him up with ropes, and robbed him of about 500 yuan in foreign currency before fleeing with a shout.

Pinghu 85

Provincial Order to Search Lu Changlang's Home

The other day, the county authorities received a secret order from the provincial government, stating that Lu Changlang, a former member of the House of Representatives from Tangji Bridge in this county, was suspected of treason and should be searched immediately. The county Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang Zhengcong was instructed to lead the entire police squad, fully armed, to surround Lu's residence on all sides and search the interior. For a time, traffic was cut off, and the... situation was terrifying. Lu was a member of the Tongmenghui in the late Qing Dynasty and was a close friend of Chen Yingren, Yao Zhiqiang, and others. In the early Republic, Yuan Shikai was in power and appointed Xu Baoshan to garrison the Songhu area. Lu designed to assassinate him by bombing him, and was subsequently wanted and fled to Japan. Later, he served as a member of the House of Representatives. When Cao Kun was elected, he fled to rely on the Extraordinary President Sun Yat-sen and participated in the Constitutional Protection Movement. After Sun Yat-sen passed away, he returned home to chant scriptures and did not participate in external affairs. Recently, with the Japanese pirates in the Northeast, his nerves became disturbed, and he scolded the east, day and night, from the... building, pointing his halberd finger. He also destroyed all the Buddha statues he worshiped. The other day, his madness flared up, and he wrote a special letter to the provincial government authorities, saying, "I have already declared myself emperor, and you should quickly choose an auspicious day to come and pay homage." The provincial authorities were unaware that he was already insane and ordered the county to search nearby. It is now known that there are no prohibited items in his home, and his son has issued a certificate confirming that he is indeed insane. Therefore, a factual report has been submitted, and for several days, teahouses and taverns have been spreading the word, making it a laughingstock.

Qingjiang 86

Provincial Huaiyin Normal School Careless

The Jiangsu Provincial Huaiyin Normal School in this city, inside the West Gate, has two playgrounds, east and west. At the south end of the west playground, there used to be a row of tile-roofed bungalows, where the school's infirmary, barber shop, and other facilities were located. Last week, the final examinations for all grades were completed, and most of the students returned home. The doors of the infirmary and other rooms were locked. Unexpectedly, today (6 PM on the 25th), a fire broke out in the infirmary due to an electrical short circuit. When people heard the alarm and rushed to the scene, the fire had already reached the roof. The school staff and the principal, etc., supervised the school workers to do their best to put out the fire, and it was finally extinguished. However, several bungalows had been burned down. Fortunately, the school's student dormitories, department classrooms, and auditorium were not affected. Principal Gu has now prepared a report and telegrammed the Education Department to report on the incident.

Brother's Brawl Turns Tragic 87

Xia Dianneng, a farmer from Liudu in the third district of Huaiyin, argued with Xia Dianbang because he refused to lend him a plow. The argument led to a fight, and Xia Dianneng was beaten on the head by the Dianying brothers with sticks. On the 24th, he was taken to the Renci Hospital outside the city for treatment, but died of his injuries. Xia Dianneng had a younger brother, Dianyang, who went to the county government to file a complaint, requesting an autopsy and prosecution. Judge Xiao went to examine the body yesterday afternoon and confirmed that he had been fatally injured by a wooden stick during his lifetime. He issued an arrest warrant for Xia Dianying and others to be dealt with according to law.

Pinghu bandits massacred each other due to uneven distribution of spoils, resulting in a firefight. Before he could escape, he was intercepted by the police and militia and sent to the county government. After interrogation, he was sent to the hospital for treatment.

National Goods Promotion Rally of the Citizens' Federation of the First Special District of Shanghai 92

National Goods Save the Nation

(Photo by Qichang Photo Studio)

Chairman's Report 93

After performing the rituals, the Presidium unanimously elected Wang Xiaolai to report, who briefly said, "This is the third time that our association has held a National Goods Promotion Rally. After repeated promotion by our association, the citizens have a considerable understanding of the need to promote national goods. Therefore, today I dare to advise you with the eight characters 'National Goods Save the Nation, Local Save the Nation.' As for promoting national goods, we must start from ourselves and then extend to our local areas. I hope that everyone will promote national goods and expand national goods so that national goods can have considerable development, and the country will gradually prosper. When the country exists, the people exist; when the country perishes, the people perish. The country and the people cannot be separated and independent. I hope that from today onwards, everyone will work together to promote and expand national goods," and so on.

Guest Speeches 94

Next, Ji Zepu, Director of the Guidance Department of the International Trade Bureau, delivered a speech entitled "Prerequisites for Promoting National Products," roughly stating that before advocating for national products, there are various issues that must be resolved first. Only then will promoting national products have a significant effect. This is what past events have told us. I will only speak briefly based on my personal observations, but what I am about to say may not be welcomed by everyone. However, for the sake of promoting the improvement of national products and increasing consumer purchasing power, I would like to speak with you in the most earnest manner. I hope there will be no misunderstandings. A. Regarding the lack of production, our country was originally an agricultural nation and has not paid much attention to industry. Since the opening of the sea borders, the loss of China's annual trade deficit has been enormous. Therefore, patriots in the country are deeply worried and realize the importance of industry. Establishing factories for self-manufacturing is the only way to counter the huge outflow of wealth. Now, factories are springing up and gradually developing, which is an excellent phenomenon. However, upon further observation, the common problem with today's Chinese industries is that, in the early stages of operation, those in charge are diligent, hardworking, and strive to conduct research, showing vigorous momentum. The products also achieve considerable results. But once money becomes abundant and business develops, they no longer deepen their research on production improvement or continue their efforts. As a result, business declines and the quality of products deteriorates. This is also an undeniable fact in the history of Chinese industry. In contrast, factories in other countries send people out to investigate various products and methods to reduce costs. People who start businesses are willing to continue to work hard and conduct research, so their businesses can take deep root. B. Inevitable jealousy among competitors is a widespread malady among Chinese merchants. This kind of mentality, planted in our hearts, is most likely to hinder the development of Chinese industry. Because of competition among the same trades, our country does not hesitate to make unnecessary sacrifices and does not know how much life and property have been lost. Therefore, there is advocacy for cooperation. I hope that Chinese people will broaden their horizons and do things based on the spirit of cooperation, only then will they have the qualifications to resist foreign goods. Otherwise, it is self-deception. International trusts formed by foreigners emphasize international cooperation and compete with other countries. For example, when Soviet Russian kerosene was promoted in China, companies such as Mobil, Asiatic Petroleum Company, and Texaco joined forces and lowered prices to compete with Soviet Russia, which was starting commercial activities. Even with different nationalities, foreigners can still cooperate. Can we not feel ashamed when we see this? C. Regarding the lack of consumption, the consumption of citizens in powerful countries is not unconscious. Everything they use is bought from their own country's products. They are never willing to easily give money to foreigners. Citizens are willing to buy goods based on this significant benefit, so the country can be strong and the people rich. Looking at the psychology and level of consumers in our country, there are many areas that are truly depressing. 1. Chinese people in general are the only consumers, because they own huge assets. Therefore, for the purchase of all enjoyment items, regardless of which country's goods they are, or what the value is, they only use the most noble and beautiful as the standard. For example, dozens of gold coins for a piece of clothing material, dozens of yuan for a pair of socks, etc. National products are naturally not welcome. How can national products be promoted when there are such consumers in the country? This is a major flaw in Chinese consumers. 2. Ordinary Chinese consumers are a large number of people with strong purchasing power, but most of them have not received sufficient education and do not know what a country is. Therefore, for the purchase of everything they use, regardless of right or wrong, or which country's goods they are, they always use low prices as the standard. Therefore, foreigners use this weakness to promote goods in large quantities. This is also a major reason why national products are not fully selling. In addition to the shortcomings of both production and consumption, there are also some merchants who worship foreigners and specialize in promoting foreign goods, changing labels and numbers. This also makes it unclear whether national products are different from foreign goods, so those who are patriotic and willing to buy them are at a loss. With such phenomena existing in the country, it is not easy to promote national products. Finally, looking at the advanced industrial countries in Europe and America, their products can be called the crown of the world, but they still think it is not enough. Therefore, for each type of product, they hold grand exhibitions and publicity conferences every year, using various unique official publicity methods to make the national people deeply aware of their country's products. Even industrially advanced countries are still working hard to publicize national products. Our country, which is backward and still in its infancy, should work harder to publicize national products, so that the national people are aware of the characteristics of the products of various factories in the country, and then sales will inevitably increase day by day and month by month. Next, Wu Zhihao, Ling Yun, Shen Tianxin, Chen Jicheng, and Cao Zhigong gave speeches successively. The speeches were long and will be omitted.

Radio Broadcast 95

Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, Mr. Yu Zhongxian used the radio to broadcast on Greater China Radio, and the topic was "The True Meaning of the National Goods Movement," roughly saying, "What I want to talk about today is the method after the national goods movement. In the world, no matter which nation, there is no one who does not practice survival of the fittest. Therefore, from September 18th of the year before last and January 28th of last year to the present, the Japanese army has been invincible in our country, advancing and occupying territory, letting them cut and carve. This is not because the Japanese army conquered us, nor is it because Japan has a large amount of military spending to conquer us, but it is because Japan's skills conquered us. The Japanese have the skills to make sophisticated guns and cannons, and can make poison gas that kills without bloodshed. We cannot make them, or are unwilling to work hard to research and manufacture sophisticated military equipment. Recently, Japan has come to provoke us, and it can be said that people with industrial manufacturing skills are conquering people without industrial manufacturing skills. We want to resist foreign goods, and at the same time, we must revitalize our own industry. If we only advise people not to buy foreign goods, and we are still lazy and unwilling to work hard to do manufacturing work, that is like climbing a tree to catch fish. We must change the two words 'resist' to 'manufacture and resist'. Everyone bury their heads in work. People with industrial skills should engage in industrial manufacturing as much as possible. People with sales skills should try their best to promote the products of national goods factories. People with the ability to buy should buy national goods as much as possible. Then, even if we don't resist foreign goods, they will have no foothold in our market. Therefore, if the country wants to be revitalized, it is necessary to promote industry. If society wants to be consolidated, it is necessary to use national goods."

Entertainment and Gifts 96

Mr. Pan Jinsheng's harmonica solo had a melodious tone and was very pleasant to listen to. Then, Zhao Zhongshan and Shen Chunlin performed magic tricks, and their movements were considered agile. Following that, all the members of the Chrysanthemum Society performed a new play with police workers, with profound implications and deeply touching. At the venue, the factories that donated products included China-Europe Candy Company's candy, Paris Cosmetics Factory's tooth powder, Yicheng Tobacco Company's exquisite round fans, Watson's and Yili Soda, and American Fresh Orange Juice Company's fresh orange juice.
