3 Million Yuan of New Currency in Circulation on July 1st 97

The alloyed color is excellent, and it will be inspected as it is cast in the future.

Certificates are printed quickly, and each box is affixed with proof of the alloyed color.

The Mint is waiting for the Ministry of Finance to order the casting of subsidiary coins.

Guowenshe reported that the Central Mint has completed a large batch of new coins. Now, it has been ordered to start circulating 3 million yuan from July 1st. The factory and the New Coin Review Committee have been actively working in recent days.

In preparation for circulation, the Central Mint, since being ordered to prepare for the casting of new coins, initially cast a small number. Later, due to their poor quality, the old molds were discarded and new models were used, removing the semi-circular sun shadow. From the new model to the present month, a large batch has been completed. Now, it is scheduled to issue 3 million new coins from July 1st to circulate in the market. In the future, they will be cast and issued at any time, and tested batch by batch. It is hoped that they will circulate throughout the country on the one hand, and gradually recover the old coins across the country on the other hand, until the old coins disappear completely and new coins are fully used.

At any time, the Central Mint hired engineer Ge Laide to come to China, and he has arrived in Shanghai to take charge of the testing work. At the same time, a testing office was also established in the New Coin Review Committee. All 3 million new coins have been tested, and the results showed that the alloyed color was completely consistent and even more excellent than expected. Therefore, a report will be submitted to the Review Committee in the middle of next month.

The circulation procedures for the 3 million new coins to be circulated have been packed into boxes. Now, the reviewers are rushing to prepare certificates, using both Chinese and Western languages, and stamped with the seal of Committee Chairman Kong Xiangxi, with one paper affixed to each box to prove its alloyed color. As for whether the issuance will be handled separately by the Central Bank or simultaneously by various banks when it starts at that time, it is still unclear.

Subsidiary Coin Issue 98

The Ministry of Finance, in order to unify the currency system, intends to order the Mint to cast decimal silver subsidiary coins and first consult the Municipal Bankers Association for opinions. The association's reply to the Ministry of Finance has been recorded in previous reports. It is now heard that the Mint has not yet received the order from the Ministry of Finance. However, regarding the issue of decimal silver subsidiary coins, the Mint has planned to proceed and is currently waiting for the order from the Ministry of Finance before preparing to start casting.

Water Fee in the Public Concession 99

There will be another dispute.

Exceeding more than 20%.

Disconnection of water is unavoidable if no contract is signed.

Xinsheng News Agency reported that the British-owned Water Company previously charged water fees according to the new rate water meter system, which was 7.5% of the rent, exceeding more than half. The owners could not afford this extra water price and stopped paying the water fees, which led to a water disconnection storm. Later, Ping Bingnan took on the role of mediator and paid the water fees, guaranteed by Huayi. Where the water was disconnected, the company sent personnel to turn on the water, and the situation was slightly eased. The Water Company temporarily set a trial method: those with a rent of more than 125 yuan would be charged 7.5 cents per 1,000 gallons, and those with a rent of less than 10 yuan would be charged 1.71 cents per 1,000 gallons. However, even with the trial use to date, calculating at 7.5% of the original rent still exceeds half. According to reports from the Real Estate Association, some have a rent of more than 20%. The Water Company believes that this delay is not good, so it urged the owner representatives of the Real Estate Association to sign a new contract to make up for the losses. However, the owner representatives believe that this water price exceeds more than 30% and it is not convenient to immediately approve it. Meetings have been held repeatedly, but there is no solution. Currently, the company and the owners are brewing a dispute. According to news from the company, if the above situation is that the owners are no longer sincere in signing the contract, then the water disconnection problem is still unavoidable.

Page 11

The Ministry of Railways Rectifies Joint Transportation 101

Detailed measures are formulated.

Implemented on July 1st.

Since the Joint Transportation Office of the Ministry of Railways has been handling the joint transportation of goods between the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways and the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, it has achieved considerable results. However, the method of payment on arrival and the method of calculating transportation costs are of great importance. The Ministry of Railways has formulated a rectification plan and implemented it on time. The details are recorded below.

Joint Transportation Payment on Arrival Method 102

The Ministry of Railways specifically telegraphed the Shanghai-Nanjing and Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration yesterday regarding the joint transportation payment on arrival method, stating that the payment on arrival method and joint transportation payment on arrival are of great importance and must be thoroughly implemented in order to provide merchants with as much convenience as possible. Otherwise, the freight transportation of each railway will not be able to fully develop, and the payment on arrival joint transportation should be actively carried out. After the implementation of the payment on arrival joint transportation, all freight charges received by the joint transportation railways must be actually collected and actually allocated. No payment should be deducted from the income from this joint transportation payment on arrival. Only then can the joint transportation payment on arrival be sustainable, and the Ministry's policy of developing freight transportation can be thoroughly implemented. After receiving the order, the Railway Administration shall order the Transportation and Accounting Departments to comply with it separately.

Method of Calculating Freight Charges 103

The Ministry of Railways investigated that since the two railways and the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Administration have been responsible for the joint transportation of goods, each joint transportation station has ignored the third decimal place when calculating freight charges, resulting in frequent errors of underpayment or overpayment when auditing freight tickets. In order to unify the method of calculating freight charges for the three railways and facilitate auditing, a standard calculation method has been formulated, and ordinary, premium, responsible, priority, and top priority items have been made into tables, compiled into a booklet, and distributed to the three railways for use, with July 1st as the implementation date.

All of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company 104

Marine engineers request a salary increase.

Same treatment as the driving department.

The bureau's reply has conditions attached.

All marine engineers on all ships of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company have jointly requested a salary increase from the bureau due to unfair treatment by the bureau. Liu Hongsheng rejected the request, and the situation has become increasingly serious. The Board of Directors has accepted this matter for review. The reporter of this newspaper will record the details of the investigation as follows.

Reasons for the Request 105

The 25 ships of the bureau, both inland and ocean-going, employ a total of 80 marine engineers. Their wages are lower than those of the driving department on each ship. The marine engineers believe that the responsibilities of driving and marine engineering are equal among the crew members. British companies such as Taikoo and Jardine also treat personnel in both departments equally. Only the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is particularly generous to the driving department's wages, while the marine department's wages are extremely meager. Now, at a time when the cost of living is rising, all marine engineers have unanimously decided to request an increase in wages in accordance with the driving department's wages, and have jointly signed and sealed a request to Manager Liu to handle it.

Status of Negotiations 106

After all marine engineers submitted the reasons for the salary increase and the comparison table of the salary amounts of the two departments to the manager and the Board of Directors, Liu Hongsheng immediately summoned the marine engineers and stated to the public that the crew's wages were not set after he took office, but were drafted by the former head of the shipping department, Yang Ying, and it was difficult to approve the requested increase. If they were dissatisfied, they could do whatever they wanted. His words were quite suggestive of rejection. All marine engineers believe that this reasonable request, if the bureau does not increase their salaries, will definitely be submitted to the Ministry and the National Government to ask for a decision. The submission is already being drafted.

General Outline of the Original Submission 107

It is believed that although the driving and marine engineering departments have their own specialized duties, their ranks are equal. The treatment of the captain, first mate, second mate, and chief engineer, first engineer, and second engineer should be the same according to the shipping companies of various countries. However, our China Merchants Steam Navigation Company discriminates against marine engineering staff in every way and treats them unequally. Now, let's just talk about wages. The monthly salary of a Chinese captain ranges from 360 yuan to 500 yuan, the first mate from 160 to 190 yuan, and the second mate from 80 to 130 yuan, while the chief engineer is only 160 to 200 yuan, the first engineer only 100 to 130 yuan, and the second engineer 80 yuan. Compared, the injustice is extreme. According to the principle, the captain and chief engineer are equally responsible for the safety of the entire ship, and there is absolutely no difference in importance or rank. Now, the chief engineer's earnings in two months are less than the captain's earnings in one month. This is one reason. Moreover, since the colleagues took office, there has never been any accident or negligence in the marine engineering department. In addition, there are very few marine engineering schools, and there is a shortage of talent. If we do not advocate and encourage and increase wages, it may affect marine engineering talent. This is very important. Moreover, appointing the virtuous and enabling the capable is valued by the shipping industry. Now, this bureau has accumulated habits over the years, only focusing on the rank of the position, without distinguishing the merits of the talent. How can we clarify the standards of promotion and demotion and prevent the advancement of those who seek good fortune? Some colleagues have been serving in the bureau for seven or eight years, but their salaries are still the same. The current cost of living is very different from the past. With such a small salary, how can we support our families? We should request that the salaries be increased in accordance with the fixed amount of the driving department, and implement the fixed practice of annual salary increases. We respectfully request that it be implemented quickly. (Omitted below)

Stages of Salary Increase 108

The amount of salary increase requested has been decided by all marine engineers in public agreement, with separate provisions for inland and ocean-going vessels, and the method of annual progressive increase is specified. (A) Ocean-going vessels: The monthly salary of the chief engineer will be increased to 260 yuan, with an annual increase of 20 yuan, up to 400 yuan. The monthly salary of the first engineer will be set at 160 yuan, with an annual increase of 15 yuan, up to 250 yuan. The second engineer will be set at 110 yuan, with an annual increase of 10 yuan, up to 150 yuan. The third engineer will be set at 80 yuan, with an annual increase of 10 yuan, up to 110 yuan. (B) Inland vessels: The chief engineer will be set at 220 yuan, with an annual increase of 20 yuan, up to 360 yuan. The first engineer will be set at 150 yuan, with an annual increase of 15 yuan, up to 210 yuan. The second engineer will be set at 100 yuan, with an annual increase of 10 yuan, up to 150 yuan. The third engineer will be set at 70 yuan, with an annual increase of 10 yuan, up to 100 yuan.

Bureau's Reply 109

Liu Hongsheng has implemented instructions for this matter, and has not outwardly rejected the request for a salary increase, but two methods have been stipulated: According to the bureau's regulations, the marine engineers must be tested according to their technical skills. Those who pass the exam will be given a discretionary salary increase. Those who only rely on experience and have no academic knowledge and cannot take the exam will be paid the original salary for the time being. The request for a universal salary increase cannot be approved. The instructions were unsatisfactory to all marine engineers and they have proceeded with the second step, submitting a public submission to the Ministry for appeal.

Joint Promulgation by the Executive Yuan 110

Detailed Rules for the Red Cross Society

丨The full text consists of forty-three articles丨

Executive Yuan President Wang Zhaoming, Minister of Interior Huang Shaoxiong, Minister of Foreign Affairs Luo Wengan, Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin, and Minister of the Navy Chen Shaokuan jointly issued an instruction to promulgate the implementation rules of the Chinese Red Cross Society in Shanghai. The full text consists of forty-three articles, which are of great importance to rescue operations in wartime and peacetime. The Xin Xin News Agency reporter has selected and excerpted the main points as follows: Article 5 states that if public land and houses are needed for the construction of association buildings and the undertaking of rescue matters, they may be given with the approval of the competent authorities. Article 7 states that if each branch has no rescue achievements within one year, personnel may be sent to supervise its progress or dissolve it. Article 8 states that local branches may cooperate with local relief agencies in carrying out relief operations. Article 9 states that, with the permission of the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ministry of the Navy, wartime sanitation services may conduct battlefield rescue exercises in advance. Article 10 states that the government may subsidize the association's funds. Article 16 states that the association may be issued donation books with the seal of the Ministry of Interior for fundraising. Article 17 states that all materials used by the association may be exempt from customs duties and all miscellaneous taxes. Article 18 states that members will be solicited once a year and fundraising will be done once a year, with the local chief executive as the chairman. Article 34 states that (1) during wartime, the association will be managed by the military commander to handle rescue matters; (2) during wartime, there will be no re-election until normal conditions are restored. Article 36 states that during wartime, monks, Taoists, nuns, or other groups may be recruited to assist. During wartime, their treatment will be the same as that of military dependents, and they may be given vehicles, ships, and hospital ships by the military commander. Article 38 states that during wartime, sanitation materials will be allocated by the military commander and reimbursed truthfully afterwards. Article 39 states that other groups engaged in sanitation in the war zone must consult with the association. Article 41 states that the staff of the Red Cross Society will be subject to the Commendation Regulations, etc. It is also learned that the Chinese Red Cross Society will be treated the same as the governments of European and American countries in the future.

Case of Tax Collection on Houses on North Szechuan Road 118

Statement from the Municipal Finance Bureau

Striving for Fair Burdens for Citizens

Those Who Resist Taxes Will Be Dealt With According to the Law

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, the Municipal Finance Bureau issued a statement yesterday by the head of the bureau, Cai, in response to the opposition from various groups in Hongkou against the municipal government's collection of house taxes. The statement from the bureau's responsible official is as follows: This bureau is in charge of all tax revenue in the city, and strives to ensure fairness in the burdens borne by citizens. The current collection of house taxes in the North Szechuan Road area is originally intended to equalize the burdens of citizens. The reasons listed by the merchants and residents there are not sufficient. (1) Regarding the so-called issue of roads built beyond the boundary, which has been unresolved for a long time, the request to postpone the payment of house taxes is unwarranted. The recovery of roads built beyond the boundary is a comprehensive diplomatic issue. The government is currently conducting negotiations on this matter. How can it be unreasonably linked to the collection of house taxes as an excuse to refuse payment of house taxes? Moreover, even before the issue of roads beyond the boundary is resolved, other matters such as telephones have been resolved one after another. It can be seen that all matters that should be handled by this city will be handled in order, complementing the negotiation for the recovery of road rights. (2) Regarding the claim that the residents in that area are a mix of Chinese and foreigners, and that the municipal government's tax collection announcement only concerns Chinese citizens and not others, which is unfair, this bureau's collection of house taxes in that area does not exclude foreign residents. For example, the Yunfei Motor Company in that area, which is originally an American business, has also been levied house taxes for this quarter, which can serve as proof. (3) Regarding the claim that the issue of boundary disputes has not been resolved, the authority cannot be unified, and citizens' tax burdens are duplicated, this bureau will not collect taxes again from citizens in the area of roads built beyond the boundary who are currently paying house taxes to the special district due to the use of utilities in the special district. All areas where the city's police force has reached and those using utilities in the city will be subject to house taxes. The method is already fair. Moreover, after this city collects house taxes, this bureau will be responsible for ensuring that citizens do not have to bear duplicate burdens. There are many citizens in that area who understand the greater good and should comply with the regulations and pay taxes, fulfilling their obligations as citizens.

According to the Central News Agency, regarding the issue of house taxes in the section of roads built beyond the boundary on North Szechuan Road, the municipal government meeting has already decided to encourage citizens to pay. According to the person in charge of the municipal government, the municipal government has decided to collect the taxes and will not change its decision. However, the method of implementing the collection is still under consideration. Those who incite or instigate tax resistance will be dealt with according to the law. Good citizens will not be arbitrarily arrested. As for the responsibility of the head of the second branch of the fifth district, an investigation is currently underway.

Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou 119

Representatives of the Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Go to Beijing to Petition

Order to Stop the Newly Revised Tax Amounts

The Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Association Joint Council is preparing to collect the newly revised fixed-amount tax on tobacco and alcohol by the Taxation Administration of the Ministry of Finance starting from July 1st. It has specially sent six representatives, including Cao Gexian, Yu Xunlu, Dai Zhuoan, Jin Yunjie, Huang Wenqing, and Huang Yuming, to Beijing to petition relevant authorities. It is learned that the representatives have entrusted lawyer Li Sanwu in Nanjing to draft a petition, which has been submitted to the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, requesting a prompt order to stop the tax. The original text states, "A petition regarding the Taxation Administration's preparation to illegally collect taxes on local tobacco and alcohol, requesting a prompt order to stop it to uphold national law and protect civil rights." Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, the domestic tobacco and alcohol industry has been using the old monopoly system. For several years, merchants have had no inconvenience. It has recently been heard that the Taxation Administration of the Ministry of Finance plans to abolish the monopoly system of salt and draft regulations such as fixed-amount taxes on local alcohol, and implement them on July 1st of this year. The Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Association Joint Council, as the matter concerns national laws and the rights of the people, has appointed Gexian and others as representatives of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou industry to petition in Beijing, requesting the suspension of implementation, and submitting a document for review. According to our country's constitution, which has not yet been enacted, the Provisional Constitution during the period of political tutelage is the fundamental law of the country. Article 25 of the Provisional Constitution states that people have the obligation to pay taxes according to law. The term "law" refers to a proposal submitted according to a certain procedure, and the principles are decided by the political conference, transferred to the Legislative Yuan, and passed through the procedures of the Legislative Yuan, and announced by the National Government. The tobacco and alcohol monopoly system occurred before the promulgation and implementation of the Provisional Constitution, which is beyond question. After the promulgation and implementation of the Provisional Constitution, any state agency wishing to reform any tax must enact a law through the Legislative Yuan and implement it accordingly. The Taxation Administration drafted regulations to collect fixed-amount taxes on local alcohol, etc. Since it is a regulation, it should have gone through the legislative procedure. Since it has not gone through the legislative procedure, it can be known that it is not a legally produced law. Since it is not a legally produced law, no matter how cumbersome, repetitive, light, heavy, unbalanced, or imaginative the content of the regulations is, whether it is retroactive or strange, wanting to put all tobacco and alcohol merchants to death, it is practically impossible to implement. Since the basis is not a law, the people have absolutely no obligation to obey. Even if a law is legally enacted, the people can still consider their ability to pay taxes, state the facts from all sides, and provide opinions for the legislators' reference in advance. How can they ignore everything, work behind closed doors, want to replace the supreme law of the country with freely drafted regulations, and force the people to obey? Gexian and others, upholding the spirit of the rule of law, do not want the government to fall into injustice. They should truthfully state their attitude and report it. All tobacco and alcohol merchants in Shanghai, Nanjing, and Suzhou will not recognize the illegal fixed-amount tax on local alcohol and special tax regulations on local tobacco leaves drafted by the Taxation Administration this time, and request the Ministry to respect national laws and the rights of the people, and immediately order the suspension of implementation, so as to avoid accidents. In the event that the Taxation Administration ignores everything and insists on going its own way, and insists on forcing the collection according to the newly drafted regulations, then all tobacco and alcohol merchants in Shanghai, Nanjing, and Suzhou still have hearts and blood, unanimously refuse to pay, and insist to the end, not hesitating any sacrifice. I think the Ministry will be able to maintain the prestige of the country and the dignity of the law, and will not allow the Taxation Administration to act presumptuously and incite misfortune. Words are urgently presented, hoping to be adopted. The matter is urgent, and there is no time to choose words. Besides submitting separately, I respectfully submit to the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance. Representatives: Cao Gexian, Yu Xunlu, Dai Zhuoan, Jin Yunjie, Huang Wenqing, Huang Yuming.

San Francisco 123

Seizure of Narcotics Shipped from Shanghai

=Found Hidden in the Bottom of Tung Oil Barrels on the Japanese Ship Asama Maru

Narcotics Worth 300,000 Yuan=

According to the Continental Daily, details have arrived in Shanghai about the case in San Francisco, USA, involving the seizure of anesthetic narcotics shipped from Shanghai, totaling US$300,000. The case was uncovered on the night of the 2nd of this month. Acting on a tip from Chinatown, San Francisco customs officers boarded the Japanese ship Asama Maru immediately after it arrived at the port and found the narcotics hidden in the bottom of tung oil barrels. According to customs officers, six shipments have been secretly transported from Shanghai recently, this being the last. On the American side, there is an international smuggling ring led by Judah Ezra and Isaac Ezra, along with a Chinese-American surnamed Zhong. The tung oil was marked as being delivered to the Donaghe Lai Company, which is also a smuggling organization set up by the Ezras. Previously, U.S. federal investigators searched a warehouse on Kansas Street on May 19 after arresting the Ezra brothers, but the oil drums with the hidden narcotics had already been shipped out. Later, they thoroughly investigated the ship's shipping manifests and other related documents but found no clues. Therefore, the seizure of a large quantity of narcotics on the Asama Maru can be said to be a major achievement in the investigation. When searching the warehouse, a small printing shop was discovered, where the Ezra brothers were printing large quantities of sign paper marked with "Three Star Morphine," "Three Star Opium," and "Made in France." Also, according to Allied, the leader of the smuggling ring's San Francisco branch, the Ezra brothers initially sold on credit to intermediaries, giving them discounts. As business expanded in the San Francisco and Los Angeles areas, they then moved on to promoting it in New York. He was arrested when he was about to go to New York to take on a new leadership role. In this incident, there were a total of eight tung oil barrels with hidden compartments on the Asama Maru, and 800 ounces of narcotics, worth a total of 300,000 yuan, were found in the bottom of two barrels. However, this is only part of the million-yuan shipment of narcotics. So far, nine people have been arrested, including two Chinese-Americans. There is also a Barris who is accused of attempting to transfer the eight barrels of tung oil with hidden compartments on the Asama Maru from San Francisco to Los Angeles.

Branch of the Bank of China at Xiaodongmen 124

11,000 Yuan Robbed

=Six Robbers Arranged Everything in Advance, Hired a Car to Wait

Unsuspecting Escort of Pig Trade Funds, Robbed by Surprise=

The Bodyguard Disarmed, the Old Clerk Powerless

The case of the 127,000-yuan robbery in the French Concession, which shocked the entire city, had just been solved by the police, when another huge robbery occurred yesterday afternoon at 2:40 PM in the Huiguan Alley on Limma Road in the Sixteen Pows of the South City. The victim was the Xiaodongmen Branch of the Bank of China, and the loss amounted to 11,000 yuan. Moreover, these robbers had arranged everything in advance. The details obtained from the investigation are recorded below.

Pig Trade Funds 125

Yong'an Lane on Limma Road in the Sixteen Pows of the South City, its front door faces Limma Road, and the back door is in the Huiguan Alley. Most of the residents in this lane are pig traders, and their business is very prosperous. The daily payment of funds is about 70,000 to 80,000 yuan. However, these funds have always been handled by the Xiaodongmen Branch of the Bank of China, which sends personnel to the lane at about 2:00 PM every day to deliver the funds separately to the pig traders. In order to avoid accidents, each time the funds are delivered, a bodyguard is sent to escort them, which is a common practice.

Bodyguard Escort 126

Yesterday afternoon at 2:30 PM, the bank sent funds as usual. However, because the bank had been notified by the pig traders in advance that there were no large amounts of funds to be paid out, the bank put 11,000 yuan in banknotes and silver dollars into a cloth bag and sent shop clerk Song Baiqing to deliver them. All the banknotes were five-yuan notes from the bank. Because Limma Road was under construction and the rickshaw could not pass, and the lane was also closed due to the construction, with everyone entering and exiting through the back door in the Huiguan Alley, the rickshaw driver Song Yunbiao was ordered to carry the cloth bag on his shoulder, led by Song Baiqing, straight to Xiangguajie, and then turn into Huiguan Alley to go to Yong'an Lane. The bodyguard Gao Shiyu escorted them along the way.

Hired Car Waiting 127

At about 1:00 PM yesterday afternoon, two men, both around 30 years old, suddenly came to the Zhonghua Motor Company on Marlborough Road in the French Concession, claiming that they wanted to rent a car to go to the South City. The motor company dispatched a car driven by Xu Guobao, with city license number 4466 and concession license number 12662, for them to ride in. When they arrived at the open space opposite the Dada Wharf on the Outer Limma Road in the South City (because the area was being renovated), the two men ordered Xu to stop the car and told him to wait there. They got out of the car and walked to Limma Road, turned into Huiguan Alley, and met with four other men who were waiting there. They lingered on the side of the road, as if they were waiting for someone.

Snatching the Cloth Bag 128

Among these six men, two were wearing white short shirts and pants, two were wearing blue silk long gowns, and the clothing of the others is unknown. When it was 2:40 PM, Song Baiqing, a shop clerk from the Bank of China, was seen turning into the alley from Xiangguajie, walking slowly. The men immediately gave a signal and swarmed forward. First, four men pinned down the bodyguard Gao Shiyu and took out pistols, threatening him not to make a sound. They took away the police whistle he carried, a white Langlin pistol, and nine bullets. At that time, Song and others knew they had encountered robbers and were stunned. Two robbers immediately rushed forward and forcibly snatched the cloth bag containing 11,000 yuan in banknotes and silver dollars from the rickshaw driver Song Yunbiao's shoulder. After getting the loot, they, together with the four robbers, ran quickly to the car that was waiting at the open space opposite the Dada Wharf. One of the robbers took out a pistol again, drove the driver Xu Guobao out of the car, and then they all got into the car and drove quickly south, with one of the robbers driving.

Searching for the Car 129

After the incident, Song Baiqing and others returned to the bank and reported to the manager. The manager immediately notified the First District Police Station by telephone. District Chief Guan Gong arrived with a large number of police officers, but because it had been a long time and the robbers were in a car and driving very fast, they could not be caught. They immediately reported the situation to the Municipal Police Bureau and ordered all district police stations to pursue the robbers. After being forced out of the car, the driver Xu Guobao returned to the motor company after his shock subsided and reported the situation. The motor company then reported to the Chinese and French police authorities, asking them to pay attention to the search for the stolen car.

Soviet Assistance Association Staff Member 144

Morrison Found Not Guilty

= Witness Proves Payment Made for Sulfite Cargo

Police Accusation of Embezzlement Cannot Be Established =

丨The Inside Story of This Case is Purely Political Manipulation丨

The Soviet Assistance Association at 2 Beijing Road is a branch of the Russian Central Consumer Cooperative. A Russian named Alexander Morrison is the director of the chemical products department of the association. In March of this year, the association shipped 298 tons of sulfite, worth 25,000 yuan, from Russia. Because there was no buyer, it was stored in the Maotai Foreign Firm warehouse. In mid-April, Xie Keming, the owner of Renji Paint Store at 1630 Guangdong Road, wanted to buy the goods. After Morrison contacted Xie several times, the transaction was completed on May 17. The association's manager, Maikefu, signed the warehouse receipt and took the goods away. However, Morrison suddenly disappeared, and Maikefu reported to the police that Morrison had embezzled the money. The police reported to the First Special District Court and issued a warrant for arrest. On June 13, Morrison suddenly surrendered to the General Patrol Room with his lawyer, Biao Fenling. The police detained him and sent him to the Special Court for interrogation and detention. Yesterday morning, Judge Qian Hongye of the Criminal Court questioned him. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated that the police were prosecuting him for embezzlement and forgery under Articles 357 and 243 of the Criminal Law, because the Association denied this sulfite transaction. The three letters of the Association contacting Renji were signed by the defendant and the accountant, Shi Lichen. Shi denied one of the signatures, claiming that it was forged by the defendant. Shi Lichen also surrendered, proving that one of the three letters was not signed by him and that the success of the transaction was unknown to the association. Maikefu testified that Morrison had told him that someone wanted to buy sulfite, but had to see the sample first in order to determine the price. Therefore, he signed the warehouse receipt. When questioned, the defendant stated that after the transaction was completed, Xie Keming signed a check and sent a bodyguard, Dong Yuqing, to accompany him in Xie's car. They first went to a money shop to get the money, and then went to the Association to hand over the money to Maikefu, and did not embezzle it. The court did not believe it and summoned Dong as a witness. Dong Yuqing testified, proving that the defendant's statement was true. The court then questioned the witnesses again and ruled that Morrison was not guilty. The police lawyer, Ru, stated that he would appeal. The court then ordered Morrison to be released on bail during the appeal period. It is said that the occurrence of this case was purely political manipulation, but neither party mentioned it during the court hearing today, so it cannot be published. After a detailed investigation, it will be reported later.

United States Silk Market Needs High-Grade Raw Silk 145

Ordinary Grade Raw Silk Floods the Market, Making it Difficult for Chinese Silk to Gain a Foothold

To Open Up Sales Channels, High-Grade Raw Silk Must Be the Vanguard

丨Report by Miao Zhongxiu After Investigating in the United States丨

The Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Silk Cocoon General Branch and the Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association jointly dispatched Miao Zhongxiu, director of the Raw Silk Inspection Department of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, to the United States to investigate the silk industry situation. When Mr. Miao passed by Japan, he sent a letter to Director Cai Wuwang, reporting on the recent situation of the Japanese silk industry. The essence of the original report was disclosed in the newspaper. Mr. Miao arrived in Seattle on May 22 and in Chicago on May 26. The director of the Raw Silk Inspection Institute accompanied him to visit spinning mills and hosiery factories near Chicago. He then reported the information he obtained in detail, which is worthy of reference for China's silk industry. Excerpts are disclosed again as follows:

Recent Trends in the American Silk Industry: The United States imports about 500,000 dan of raw silk annually, of which more than 50% is sold to hosiery factories, and the rest is purchased by various silk factories. In recent years, silk factories have used a large amount of rayon, and the raw silk they use is mostly medium-grade factory silk. However, hosiery factories use very little rayon, and most of the raw silk they use is high-quality goods. Therefore, hosiery factories play a very important role in the American silk industry. The trend of silk prices is generally optimistic. It has recently been raised to $1.75 per pound, and it is hoped that it will rise to $3. It is possible to reach above $2. There have also been many improvements in raw silk inspection methods and machinery. For example, in uniformity inspection, the 9-meter inspection (measuring uniformity by weight) has recently been adopted to supplement the black board inspection. The black board machine has also been improved and perfected, and an electric light inspection uniformity has been invented to replace visual inspection.

Reasons for the Failure of Chinese Silk and Its Rescue: Sales of Chinese silk in the United States have plummeted. From June of last year to May of this year, only over 10,000 bales were sold. Factories that used to buy Chinese silk have recently switched to Japanese silk. The reason is that the quality of Chinese silk is inconsistent. For example, the Purple Dragon brand of the Hangzhou Silk Factory was exclusively used by the largest hosiery factory in the United States several years ago because its uniformity was above 90 points. The silk stockings woven from it were very profitable. Factories competed to buy it, and demand exceeded supply. Later, Qianli Foreign Firm managed to buy 20 dan, and after other hosiery factories tried it, they were greatly disappointed. The inspection result was only 75 points of uniformity. At the same time, the first hosiery factory that purchased it also stopped purchasing it. However, American hosiery factories are still very willing for China to supply the highest-grade factory silk, that is, uniformity above 90 points, because the nature of Chinese raw silk is firmer, and the female workers are accustomed to paying attention to the strips, unlike Japanese female workers who pay attention to uniformity and ignore the strips. Often, the same 90-point raw silk can produce Chinese silk that is equivalent to 92-point Japanese silk. Therefore, if Chinese silk wants to open up sales channels in the United States, it must use high-purity raw silk as the vanguard to be able to save it. As for ordinary grade raw silk, it floods the market, and Chinese silk has no room to gain a foothold. This is what China's silk industry should be aware of.

New Beijing Steamer Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 146

Strike Wave Appeased by Ningbo Seamen's Union

According to Xinsheng News Agency, in the case of the strike of the Tai Gu Company's Nan Hua and other ships in Guangzhou, the Shanghai-Ningbo line's New Beijing steamer also experienced a strike at 5 PM the night before last. Fortunately, the Ningbo Seamen's Union sent personnel to persuade the workers of various departments of the ship, instructing them to continue sailing as usual until they received a reply from the Shanghai Union. The workers then moved the unloaded goods onto the ship and set sail at 7 PM, arriving in Shanghai yesterday morning. According to the Taikoo Company, the report of more than 20 Taikoo steamships on strike for several days is not entirely consistent with the facts. It was found that the Guangzhou side was only due to the slowdown of dock workers, so the incoming ships could not load and unload goods. The sailors and stokers of the various ships have been guests of the company for many years, and their feelings are harmonious. They still serve as usual. The ship's employees are not on strike. Ships such as Shandong, Xinjiang, Jinan, and Jinhua have all returned to Shanghai one after another, which is proof.

The Shanghai Shipping Association does not approve of the slowdown of the Guangzhou workers. Yesterday, it sent a telegram to the Guangzhou and Shantou Seamen's Unions to persuade them. The original telegram said, "Sent to Guangzhou and Shantou, and forwarded to the Ningbo Seamen's Union for your consideration. The bad habits of teahouses are known throughout the country. After the Taikoo limited salary system was ordered by the Party Department and the Ministry of Communications, it was implemented uniformly for Chinese ships. The Seamen's Union and shipping companies have always been very harmonious, and it is especially inappropriate to expand the situation due to teahouses. Please ask your chamber of commerce to find a way to eliminate it, and hope that your union will not go to extremes. Yu Hede, Chairman of the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association."

According to the New Beijing steamer, which was reported in the newspapers yesterday to have stopped sailing, with the workers and sailors unanimously slowing down work and moving the ship to the outer wharf to express their determination, the ship urgently stated that the ship has never been interrupted in its service between Shanghai and Ningbo, which shows that the New Beijing is still sailing as usual and no slowdown has occurred.

Chinese Merchants' No. 3 Circular Tram 147

Axle Breaks, Derailment, Two Cars Collide Violently

= Platform and Other Places Damaged, Significant Losses

Fortunately, Passengers Were Not Injured, Traffic Was Interrupted for a Long Time =

Chinese Merchants' Tram Company's No. 47 car on the No. 3 circular route, which runs around the city, suddenly had a wheel axle break and derail at about 10:40 yesterday morning near Dadongmen, and then collided with No. 41 car on the No. 3 route, causing significant losses. The details are divided as follows:

Axle Break, Derailment, Collision with Neighboring Car 148

Chinese Merchants' No. 47 circular tram on the No. 3 route was traveling from west to east at about 10:40 yesterday morning, and the passengers were still crowded. When it reached Dadong Station, the wheels suddenly vibrated and the car body tilted. All the passengers in the car were suddenly extremely panicked. The driver immediately stopped the car to check and found that the front wheel axle of the car had suddenly broken and detached, leaving the track. He immediately asked the passengers to get off the car and reported to the company, intending to drive back to the factory for repair. However, he still tried to drive. At first, it only made a creaking sound and there was no major problem. Unexpectedly, when it drove about 100 yards away from Xiaodongmen, No. 41 circular tram on the No. 3 route suddenly came from the opposite side on another track. At that time, the driver thought that the track was double-tracked and there was no relationship, so he continued to drive as usual, but he did not know that the wheel axle of the car had broken and was swaying while driving. Then, with a crash, the trailer of No. 41 and the front of No. 47 collided violently. At that time, No. 47 car was in danger of overturning and stopped immediately, but both cars were heavily damaged. Fortunately, no passengers were injured.

Inspecting Losses, Traffic Interrupted 149

After the incident, the ticket sales drivers checked tickets and other items to inspect the destroyed items. The iron door of the trailer of No. 41 was completely destroyed, bent, and could no longer be used. The iron door of the platform of No. 47 car was also slightly damaged, the front iron plate of the car was completely damaged, the front headlight was broken, the road sign fell off, the floor of the platform was broken, several pieces of glass were broken, and other scattered items were lost, causing significant losses. However, because only the iron door of the trailer of No. 41 car was damaged, it continued to drive as usual. After the incident, in addition to reporting to the company to find a way to tow it back, the destroyed items were also sorted out. For a time, other vehicles arrived one after another and were blocked from advancing, accumulating to

more than 20 vehicles. The Public Security Bureau also specially dispatched police officers to maintain order and direct traffic. At 11:30, the company sent craftsmen to find a way to connect other vehicles and tow them into the factory for repair, and traffic began to resume.

Responsibility for False Fire Alarms

Will Be Severely Punished for Crimes Endangering Public Safety

According to National News Agency, since the installation of automatic telephones in the city, the fire extinguishing associations have repeatedly received false fire alarm calls. They requested the authorities to investigate and deal with them strictly and find ways to stop them. After receiving the report, the Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a notice yesterday, saying, "Recently, unscrupulous people have been using automatic telephones to falsely report fire alarms, causing the fire extinguishing associations to run back and forth for no reason. This kind of behavior not only hinders fire prevention, but also disrupts public safety and should be strictly prohibited to maintain fire prevention and ensure local safety. In the future, if any of the above-mentioned situations occur again, once caught, they will be severely punished in accordance with the regulations on endangering public safety and will never be tolerated. In addition to ordering the various district teams to investigate and arrest them strictly, the public is hereby notified."

Taxpayer Association Sent a Letter to the Municipal Council 156

Requesting Exemption from Increased License Fees for the Restaurant Industry

The Chinese Taxpayer Association of the Public Settlement sent a letter to the General Office of the Municipal Council yesterday, saying, "Respectfully, we have received a letter from the Shanghai Restaurant Industry Association, stating that Li Jinhai, the owner of Xinghualou, reported that he had received a letter from the Municipal Council, stating that from July 1 of this year, the license fee would be 140 yuan per quarter. It was found that Xinghualou originally paid 45 taels of silver per quarter, but it was suddenly changed to 140 yuan per quarter, an increase of more than double. At a time when the commercial and industrial economy is sluggish, increasing taxes will be difficult for merchants and people to bear. They requested that the matter be transferred for negotiation and prevention. It was found that this case was previously sent to your council for negotiation and prevention in May 1931. On June 1, 1931, your council replied, 'In reply, your letter of May 18 regarding the tavern license fee has been noted. The Municipal Council has not yet obtained our council's consent for the new regulations on the license fee. In addition to writing to the Municipal Council, requesting that the old regulations be followed, we are replying accordingly. We hope that you will investigate and take action.' Having received this, we ordered the members to investigate. The collection of donations and taxes in the Public Settlement should be effective after being approved by the Chinese Taxpayer Association. The Chinese and Western Taxpayer Associations should be treated equally, but we do not know whether this increase in donation has been approved by your association. If it has not been approved, please ask your association to find a way to prevent it in order to provide relief and alleviate the suffering. Please also inform us so that we can follow the rules. We also received a letter from the Shanghai Western Restaurant Industry Association, stating that the members of our industry association, such as Xin Licha Western Restaurant, reported to the association that on the 20th of this month, a letter was received from the Donations Office of the Public Settlement, stating that from July 1 of this year, the business donation (license fee) for Western restaurants would be increased to 140 yuan per quarter. We are afraid that this has not been widely known, so we are notifying you accordingly. We are shocked and ask you to convene a meeting quickly. Our association immediately convened a meeting of all the members of our industry and discussed and resolved that since the city was affected by the January 28 War, not only has the national vitality not recovered, but the suffering of the citizens is even deeper. All industries are in decline and the market is deserted, especially our industry. As a result, many businesses have closed down and ceased operations. Our members already feel unable to bear the various donations and taxes that they previously owed. Now the Donations Office of the Municipal Council does not observe the business situation, does not understand the people's sentiments, and suddenly increases the business donation (license fee) from 45 taels of silver (63 yuan) per quarter to 140 yuan, which is more than double the original amount. Such harsh taxes are difficult to bear. If we do not ask the various agencies and public organizations in the city to assist in exempting us from the additional donations, we can only wait for death. Based on this, our industry association is especially asking your association to uphold justice, argue on the basis of reason, and ask the Donations Office of the Municipal Council to withdraw its order, exempt us from the additional donations, and maintain the difficulties of the merchants and show fairness. Please reply to us, and we will appreciate it. Since the city of Shanghai was invaded by enemy troops, it has been in a very desolate state, which is a fact that no one can deny. The restaurant industry is a wealthy business, which is known to everyone with common sense. This is a matter of fact and it cannot increase its burden. Furthermore, the taxpayers' meeting decided that taxes should be increased this year. This is a matter of law and it cannot increase its burden. Taxes should be sought from profits. There is no reason to drain the pond to catch the fish. Now, the restaurant industry is having difficulty maintaining its business operations and expenses. Not asking for a reduction in donations already shows a deep understanding of the overall situation. Increasing the burden again goes against the principles of taxation. Based on the letter above, we are respectfully asking your bureau to reconsider and not make the industry worse off."

Travel Business License Tax 157

The Municipal Council Agrees to Exempt Half of the Increase

Industry Colleagues Express Reluctant Acceptance

Since the Shanghai Municipal Council in the Public Concession notified the increase in the travel business license tax, it has aroused opposition from colleagues in the industry. The Shanghai Travel Business Association led the organization of the Shanghai Travel Business Anti-Public Concession License Tax Increase Committee. The details have been recorded in previous reports. Now it is learned that since the establishment of the association, it has been actively working. First, it sent detailed letters to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and the Chinese Taxpayers' Association, explaining the current business situation and the reasons and facts for the difficulty in increasing taxes, seeking assistance. Then, Sun Qiuping, Chen Wenda, Xu Wenzhao, Zhang Yichen, and Yao Songnian were sent to the Municipal Council's Donation Office to argue based on reason. After a long debate, the council agreed to temporarily reduce half of the increased amount for the autumn and winter seasons of this year. However, starting next year, the full increase would still be required without any reduction. The representatives expressed deep dissatisfaction with the continued increase next year and requested assistance from Chinese Directors Yu Qiaqing and Yuan Lvdeng, as well as Mr. He Dekui from the Municipal Council's Chinese Affairs Office. After negotiations between Yu, Yuan, He, and the Municipal Council, the council agreed to collect half of the increased amount from now on, without a time limit. The association considered the matter to be of great importance and whether to accept it would require a decision by the general assembly. Therefore, yesterday afternoon at 2:00 p.m., a general assembly of colleagues was held at the Jiangsu Hotel in Ziyoufang, Guangdong Road. Chairman Sun Qiuping presided over the meeting. After discussing the matter, it was decided to reluctantly accept the half-reduction plan and to abolish the Anti-Tax Increase Committee organization from now on. However, it was hoped that the Municipal Council would restrict the issuance of travel business licenses to avoid excessive increases in the number of colleagues and maintain business. Deep gratitude was expressed to Yu Qiaqing, Yuan Lvdeng, He Dekui, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, and the Chinese Taxpayers' Association for their strong support. At that time, travel businesses that had not joined the Travel Business Association were moved by the association's leadership in leading the industry, sparing no effort, and vigorously defending legal rights. Therefore, they requested to join the association one after another.

Master Shen Lin Yu and His Wife Are Returning to China 158

Mr. Shen Linyu is a native of Wuxian County, Jiangsu Province, and the son of Mr. Shen Zhisheng, the document director of the Bank of China in Shanghai. He received his family education from a young age. At the age of twelve, he graduated first in his class from Meixi Elementary School, and then passed the entrance exam into the second year of Tsinghua Middle School in Beijing, also in first place. He was regarded as a child prodigy. In 1923, after graduating from Tsinghua, he was sent to the United States to study political economy, banking, company management, and other subjects at Oberlin College, and was proficient in German. After graduating in three years, he obtained a bachelor's degree. He then entered the graduate school of Harvard University and obtained a master's degree in business after three years. He worked as the manager of the Chinese Import Department at a company in Iowa. He was sent by the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce as a commercial investigator stationed in the United States, and he traveled to various states in the United States to conduct on-the-spot investigations of commercial conditions, making many contributions. He has also written many books and articles in newspapers and magazines. His knowledge and experience are extremely rich. He has been in the United States for ten years. His wife, Ms. Xie Hui from Zhifu, is also a graduate of Oberlin College, majoring in social education and other subjects. She is excellent in both Chinese and Western literature. This time, the couple traveled to the western United States and participated in the Chicago Exposition. Then they will take the Empress of Canada from Vancouver to return to China. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai in early July. In the future, they will use what they have learned to serve the society, which will be of great help. It is said that the business and academic circles are vying to hire them, and several places are in contact.

Jiangxi Xiushui 161

New Contributions from the Tea Improvement Farm

| Invention of Tea Making Machinery |

The Tea Improvement Farm, jointly established by the Shanghai and Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureaus of the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute of the Ministry of Industry, is located in Baipengkeng, Xiushui, Jiangxi. Since its opening in April this year, it has been actively carrying out its duties. It is now reported that the farm's first tea has been transferred to Shanghai. Major tea merchants and tea-buying foreign firms have evaluated the color, aroma, and taste of the black tea, and all are excellent. The best can be compared with Indian and Sri Lankan black tea, and the second best is not inferior to Qihong. The farm, considering that the original equipment was not very complete, has spared no effort in improving and researching tea-making machinery. In addition to the green tea machinery designed and manufactured by Commissioner Wu Juenong and Commissioner Fang Hanzhou, which has been transported to the farm for trial use and has achieved excellent results, the farm's director, Mr. Yu Haiqing, and technician, Mr. Feng Shaoqiu, have designed and manufactured a type of black tea withering machine. It uses a circular cylinder made of copper wire mesh, installed on an iron frame at a suitable angle, with a fan placed below to pass hot air, so that the temperature inside the cylinder is maintained at around 45 degrees Celsius. The fresh leaves fall into the cylinder from the funnel opening and rotate freely. After sensing the temperature, the leaves become soft and automatically flow out from the tail of the machine, which is extremely convenient. The machine was tested on-site on the 14th of this month. The withered leaves were no different from those dried in the sun. If this is the case, the difficulty that China has had for many years in not being able to manufacture black tea in rainy weather will be solved once and for all.

Intention to Sell Heroin Conviction 164

Li Bangjie from Tianjin, at about 11 o'clock the night before, was carrying two taels of heroin on a public bus when he was stopped by Chinese Constable No. 2370 and Indian Constable No. 236 on Broadway Road. Seeing that his behavior was suspicious, they intercepted him, searched him, and found the heroin. They then took him to the Hongkou Police Station. When questioned, Li Bangjie's confession was evasive. After Judge Wu Zehan verified the confession clearly, he sentenced Li Bangjie to six months of imprisonment for intending to sell and possess opium substitutes, and two months of imprisonment for the crime of escape, to be served concurrently for seven months. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be deducted at two days for one day of imprisonment, and the evidence was confiscated.

Conviction for Shooting the Owner of an Incense Shop 165

Zhu Sentenced to Fifteen Years Imprisonment

Chen Zhikui, a 19-year-old Ningbo native and the owner of the Qianfengtai Incense Shop at the intersection of Dongxin Bridge Street and Caishi Street in the French Concession, was shot and killed in the alley next to the shop at 9 p.m. on April 14th of this year. At the same time, Chen Qiancheng, the shop's accountant, heard the sound and rushed out to rescue him and was also shot and injured. The case was investigated by Jin Jiulin, the special investigation supervisor of the French Police Department, who arrested the criminal, Zhu Quanxing (20 years old) from Wuxi, on the morning of the 13th of last month at No. 40, Shuangguili, Dushifu Road. Two white Langlin pistols and six ball bullets were found in the grass field of the Siming Guild Tomb outside the back door of No. 7, Yuqingli, Balichiao Road. He was sent to the First Special District Local Court, and the police lawyer filed a public prosecution for murder under Article 285, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. The family of the victim, the mother of the deceased, Chen Zhengshi, also hired lawyer Huang Yiyan as her agent to request an incidental private prosecution to recover losses and expenses for the support and education of the orphans, totaling 3,500 yuan. The defendant hired lawyer Zhu Dianqing to defend him. The interrogations and confessions have been recorded in previous reports. After the interrogations were concluded, the sentencing date arrived yesterday. At 10 a.m., the police sent the defendant to the court, where Judge Xiong Huiping presided over the First Criminal Court. After a brief interrogation, the judgment was announced: Zhu Quanxing was sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment for murder. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be deducted at two days for one day of imprisonment. Two pistols and six ball bullets were confiscated. For the private prosecution part, Zhu Quanxing should compensate Chen Zhengshi for losses of 500 yuan. During the appeal period, the defendant will be transferred to the detention center.

For every purchase of Wuzhou brand products worth one yuan, or foreign brand products worth two yuan, one gift will be given. Therefore, customers are rushing to buy. All those who receive gifts are extremely satisfied. Educational News

Important News 172

The Ministry of Education Promulgates Measures to Prevent Students

Changing Their Names and Surnames 173

(Nanjing, 28th) The Ministry of Education approved the Ministry of Interior's communication to the various bureaus and promulgated the revised measures to prevent students from changing their names and surnames as follows: 1. Students at all levels of schools who apply to change their names, surnames, or add surnames in accordance with Articles 2 and 30 of the revised rules promulgated by the Ministry of Interior shall, for students in schools above the junior college level, submit their applications through the school principal to the Ministry for approval. For students in schools below the secondary level, applications shall be submitted through the school principal to the local educational administrative authority for approval. A certificate of guarantee from the guarantor of admission must be added to the application, and other documentary evidence may be required if necessary. 2. Graduates of all levels of schools who apply to change their names, surnames, or add surnames, in addition to complying with the rules revised and promulgated by the Ministry of Interior, must obtain a certificate from the original school or the educational administrative authority where the original school is located (limited to cases where the original school has been discontinued). 3. When submitting the application for verification, one of the exhibits should be presented to the Ministry of Interior for approval. The original school should then submit or forward the application to the Ministry for record (however, for elementary school graduates, the original school should forward the application to the provincial and municipal educational administrative authorities for record).

(Zhenjiang, 28th) Shen Zhensheng, the principal of Rugao Provincial Normal School, and Zhu Weilin, the director of moral education, have been released. On the 28th, they came to the province to receive the press and recounted the ordeal of being arrested.

The Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center Will Hold 180

Scholarships and Financial Aid

The Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center has provisions for academic awards and tuition loans. After its establishment, it drafted two types of rules for scholarships and financial aid. These rules were revised and approved at the first meeting of the board of directors a few days ago. It is learned that the center is currently rushing to complete various procedures in preparation for holding the first scholarship and financial aid program during the summer vacation. The rules are listed below. The detailed procedures will be announced by the center separately.

Scholarship Rules 181

Article 1. The Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center establishes scholarships to promote academic research, promote culture, and reward scientific inventions and specialized writings. Article 2. The amount of the scholarship shall be determined by the board of directors according to the center's financial situation. Article 3. The center may, for the purpose of handling scholarship affairs, appoint several persons from the president of the board of directors to organize various committees to handle the affairs. Article 4. Any group or individual that donates more than 5,000 yuan to the center for scholarships will be a member of the Scholarship Fund Committee. The group may nominate one person as its representative. Article 5. Any group or individual that donates more than 20,000 yuan to the center for scholarships may designate the scope of the scholarship and冠其名於獎學金之上，名曰某某獎學金，並為獎學金基金委員會之當然委員，其團體得自推一人為代表。

冠 its name above the scholarship, naming it the "So-and-so Scholarship," and will be a member of the Scholarship Fund Committee. The group may nominate one person as its representative. Article 6. All scholarships issued by the center, except those specified in the preceding article, shall be called the Sun Yat-sen Scholarship. Article 7. The scope of the center's awards is tentatively set as the following two items: (A) scientific inventions that have been reviewed and determined by the center to be of real value; (B) specialized writings that have been reviewed and determined by the center to be of real value. Article 8. The distribution of the annual scholarship amount, except for those whose scope is designated by the donors, shall be distributed by the center according to the following percentages: (A) scientific inventions, accounting for 50 percent; (B) specialized writings, accounting for 50 percent. Article 9. Within the scope specified in Article 7, in addition to being introduced by the founders and directors of the center, groups or employers may submit applications to the center with supporting documents for inventions or writings. Article 10. The center shall handle scholarships twice a year, once every six months. Article 11. The procedure for handling scholarships is to submit the inventions and writings introduced by the founders and directors and applied for by groups or individuals to the preliminary review committee organized by the center for review. Article 12. After passing the preliminary review, it shall be submitted to the specialized review committee organized by the center for final review. Article 13. After passing the review by the specialized committee, the center shall distribute the scholarships separately on a regular basis. Article 14. For any special inventions or creations, in addition to awarding scholarships, the center may request the government to commend them. Article 15. Application regulations and other detailed rules shall be determined separately. Article 16. These rules may be amended at any time if there are any omissions. Article 17. These rules shall be implemented upon approval by the board of directors.

Hulbert Deden Eliminated on the Second Day, Panley Suddenly Defeated 183

丨Top British Player丨Beaten by South African Fagua Sheng

(Reuters dispatch from London, 27th) Today is the second day of the Hulbert Deden grass court tennis tournament. The weather is mild, and the number of spectators is quite large. Unexpected events also occurred today. The top British player, Panley, was eliminated by the young South African Fagua Sheng, which was a great surprise. Vanse was also nearly defeated by the young northern England player England. Austin eliminated Browning from France, but Panley was unexpectedly eliminated.

Noah, a young South African from Cambridge University and a student of Fagua Sheng, created a sensation today. In the second week of the men's singles, he defeated the top British player Panley with scores of 7 to 5, 6 to 1, 3 to 6, 4 to 6, and 6 to 4.

Panley was at a Loss. Fagua Sheng's ball skills are astonishing, with powerful serves and heavy forehand and backhand shots. In the first and second sets, he constantly advanced to the net, applying pressure, and then finished with heavy shots, leaving Panley at a loss, appearing like a second-rate player.

Forcing the Enemy to Retreat. In the second and fourth sets, Panley took full advantage, and his cross-court shots were successful, preventing Fagua Sheng from approaching the net. However, in the final fifth set, the South African youth repeated his previous technique, forcing his way to the net and blocking Panley's sharp return shots.

Dramatic First Set. Fagua Sheng took an early lead with a score of 3 to 0, but Panley tied it. Fagua Sheng then used an amazing overhead smash to make it 5 to 3. In the final point of the set, he lost it due to a foot fault. At 5 to 4, he lost three consecutive points after Panley retook it, making it 5 to 5, and eventually lost 5 to 7.
