Spring and Autumn Nudism

By Baihe

Some say that clothing serves the purpose of "warding off cold" and "warding off heat." Therefore, in cold weather, one should wear "wool" to ward off external cold, and in hot weather, one should wear "flannel" to ward off external heat. Others say that humans inherently possess the "ability to resist cold and heat." In ancient times, our ancestors did not wear clothes or hats, yet they lived for two or three hundred years. Later, when people started wearing clothes, human skin became unable to withstand the invasion of sunlight and rain, and "resistance" gradually declined, leading to a shortening of human lifespan. Both theories have "irrefutable" reasons, yet they are fundamentally "contradictory."

Some say that clothing signifies "humans are not beasts," hence the understanding of etiquette and the wearing of clothes and hats. Police officers arrest "bare-chested individuals," fining them two yuan and providing them with a undershirt to warn them against "offending public decency." Smoking or spitting in trams is blatantly disregarded despite strict prohibitions, but "bare-chested individuals," though not explicitly "forbidden from riding," are often chased off by ticket sellers because they are too "uncivilized." Others say that concealing sexual organs within clothing creates an inexplicable mystery around the "reproductive organs," which are merely one of the organs on the human body alongside "ears, eyes, mouth, and nose," leading to all kinds of "sexual" sins. If everyone were naked, with everyone having sexual organs just as everyone has ears, eyes, mouth, and nose, no one would be surprised. Both theories are "well-reasoned," yet fundamentally "contradictory" and incomprehensible.

In recent years, thanks to the influence and education of "foreigners" and "upper-class Chinese," everyone has gradually come to understand the grand principle that "nudity" is not only "unhygienic" but also "utterly uncivilized." However, the "nudity movement," promoted to "increase the body's resistance" and "eliminate the mystery of sexual organs," is spreading from Hong Kong to Shanghai. Amidst these "extreme" yet "unique" theories, should we "well-dressed" Shanghainese be "decently attired" or "stark naked"? It is indeed a matter of much hesitation.

The Third Great Event

By Zhen Xun

Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Committee, recently spoke at the 6th graduation ceremony of Central University, representing the Central Party Headquarters. He mentioned Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, urging people not to seek high office but to accomplish great deeds. He then analyzed the major events of the time, stating that besides the two major issues of resisting Japan and suppressing bandits, a third major event had arisen. The thousands of listeners in the Central Auditorium could not immediately figure out what the third major event was, until, after a considerable pause, he revealed that it was the problem of flood control. Currently, floods are frequently reported, and disasters are looming. Rivers are already lapping at the banks, which is the most eye-catching event in the newspapers!

This third major event is not only a concern for our well-being but also the greatest fatal wound to this dying nation! Because floods are not only merciless but also devoid of any rationality. One can still seek peace with the enemy, but there is no possibility of compromise or surrender to floods. If the floods create a situation of collapse and inundation as they did in 1931, enacting the second act of tragedy, then China, no matter how large, and its people, no matter how numerous, will probably be unable to withstand such turmoil again. Four hundred million people—this is the old statistic. The actual number today, when truly calculated, will certainly be considerably discounted. Whether this discount will become even smaller in the future is something only heaven knows!

Fortunately, the Chinese people possess the spirit of "making big things small." As the saying goes, "Turning big problems into small ones, and small problems into nothing." There are probably quite a few people with such skills today. As long as someone "enlightens" them, why be alarmed? Suppose this third major event occurred last year as well, and the National Crisis Conference designated it as one of the three major issues. By the time the conference closed, hadn't it already been forgotten? What kind of major event is this? Perhaps the newspapers are exaggerating!

The Arrogance of a Traitor

By Wang Yu

Those assembled in Changchun after the September 18th Incident are invariably labeled as traitors or puppets in our writings; even calling them "pseudo" is considered the most calm and rational approach. However, these figures are quite arrogant themselves. People like Zheng Xiaoxu compare themselves to meritorious ministers of the restoration or founding fathers. Xi Qia even said to others, "Who is the traitor? Wait and see in half a year!" Meaning that they are genuinely building a nation and will have achievements to show in half a year, without compromising any sovereignty. Those who claim to save the nation while secretly betraying countless national rights are the real traitors! This was naturally said by the chief puppet, Puyi, shortly after arriving in Changchun. Later, the reality turned out to be completely different. Xi Qia could not help but resent Japan for going back on its word, but he could not speak it out and could only harbor the resentment in his heart forever. I once saw several old newspapers published outside the customs that happened to contain two heptasyllabic poems by Zheng Xiaoxu. One was "Celebrating Chen Baochen's Birthday," which read: "Heaven turns the desolate desert into a divine capital, the elder statesman's arrival from the east startles the world. At eighty-five, he is truly a hero, seeing the elders on the half-month of the Double Ninth Festival. The strategy of restoration relies on long-term plans, the heroes of the north await the alliance of the leader. The fine cursive poems occasionally emerge, knowing the duke does not diminish the old sentiments." The other was "Thoughts on the Double Ninth Festival," which read: "In my prime, I still remember being exiled to the southern wilderness, escaping to the empty tung tree and cherishing my graying temples. How can I willingly be a forgotten elder in self-imposed exile? Who will share my soberness on this Double Ninth Festival? Chrysanthemums are not seen, autumn is colorless, the geese's messages are always late, the sea has become a mulberry field! Surely there are remnants of the previous dynasty thinking of their old master, climbing high and trying to call to the heavens." How arrogant it is! Not only does he call himself an "elder statesman" whose "arrival from the east startles the world," but because he "cannot willingly be a forgotten elder in self-imposed exile," he anticipates that "surely there are remnants of the previous dynasty thinking of their old master." In reality, who other than old fools like Zheng Xiaoxu has Puyi in their minds? Some also say that Zheng Xiaoxu and his ilk initially regarded Japan as the Khitans, thinking that Shi Jingtang could easily be emulated. Who knew that in reality, they were not even as good as Liu Yu. Liu Yu was made emperor by the Jin people in the fourth year of the Jianyan era of the Song dynasty, with the state name of Great Qi, and the capital at Daming Prefecture. He repeatedly led the Jin people to invade, but it was unsuccessful. The Jin people disliked him and eventually deposed him. But Liu Yu still illegitimately held the throne for eight years and was much more free and happy than Puyi. How could Puyi compare to Liu Yu?

Deep Water, Scorching Fire—A Desperate Situation for the People

By Zhurongshi

The scorching sun is pressing down, and summer is fearsome. The earth's temperature gradually soars with the thermometer. These days, fashionable terms like "summer retreat" and "escaping the heat" are coming into use. Places like Guling, Putuo, and Moganshan are now filled with many people's footprints. The coolness and tranquility of the mountains can indeed alleviate the heat, but for us poor commoners, who struggle to make ends meet, we can only endure the scorching of the Red Emperor and sigh at the mountains!

"As fire deepens, as heat intensifies," this is the saying of ancient sages used to describe the suffering of the people. Unfortunately, in today's society, this is perfectly accurate. Countless innocent people are being buried in water and fire. This year, the terrifying floods are already before our eyes. Floods are rampant everywhere, and countless people in various provinces are trapped in the mud. It is said that in the Jiujiang area, the floodwaters have risen sharply, and many people are fleeing to Mount Lu to escape the floods. Even families with some means are helping the old and carrying the young to climb the mountain. The famous resort for escaping the heat has been transformed into a place for escaping the flood, which is extremely ridiculous. However, the poor commoners look at the high mountains but cannot climb them, suffering immensely. The administrative authorities should consider how to help the people escape from water and fire and reach a place of comfort and safety. This is an urgent matter that cannot be delayed for a moment.

He Jian, the chairman of Hunan Province, gave a very poignant speech about the floods. He said: Natural disasters are inevitable throughout history and in all countries, but according to the comments of ancient Chinese scholars, natural disasters are related to the virtues of the ruling authorities. Therefore, he believes that the floods in Hunan Province are due to his own lack of virtue and his inability to inspire auspiciousness and eliminate the disasters. He feels extremely ashamed. We certainly express our admiration for Chairman He's remarks, but the blood of humans is too cold. If everyone could feel shame when faced with problems, the country would not be in such a terrible state. Alas! The commoners in deep water and scorching fire will soon be wiped out.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

By Zhang Henshui

Chapter Ten: Hearing the Words Alarms the Fair Heart, Vain is the Hope of Ennoblement; Listening to the Songs Reveals Yearning, Idle is the Body Serving the Country

Guizhi said, "Isn't everyone like this? I don't smoke either." Old Mother Liu said, "Your mother smokes." Guizhi said, "She can only afford to smoke a little Guandong tobacco leaf." "I don't like the smell, so my mother doesn't smoke anymore." As Old Mother Liu spoke, she became more intimate. She sat down on a broken chair by the pit, nodded, and said, "It's not easy for you two to live like this. I heard a family moved into the backyard next door. What do they do?" Guizhi thought to herself that this was her chance and said, "It's a company commander." Old Mother Liu said, "Another soldier. Do they have children?" Guizhi smiled and said, "He doesn't have any family yet. An old man and a servant live there. The company commander comes back every few days, but it's very quiet." Old Mother Liu said, "How old is the old man?" Guizhi said, "Probably over sixty, right?" Old Mother Liu sighed and said, "Why would he let his son be a soldier at such an old age?" With just this sentence, there was no need to ask anything else. It was clear that Old Mother Liu was completely dissatisfied with being a soldier. She smiled and said, "It's not easy to rise from a soldier to a company commander. He relies on his son for food, drink, clothing, and housing. What do you mean by saying it's not good?" Old Mother Liu said, "Of course, it's not easy to rise to the rank of company commander. But if a soldier rises to this level, he's probably held his head in his hands countless times. That's why I say don't let your son be a soldier." Guizhi was just about to ask a question when she heard someone cough lightly outside the window. Old Mother Liu smiled and said, "Is that Mr. Niu? Please come in, I have something to ask of you." She said as the coughing sound came from outside the door again, and then that Mr. Niu walked in. Guizhi saw that he was an old man nearing sixty. He was wearing an iron-gray cotton robe with a row of unbuttoned buttons at the hem. He was wearing a black cotton mandarin jacket over his upper body, also with the chest open. Here, one could see countless oil and wine stains and burn marks on the chest of his cotton robe. He was wearing a three-piece leather hat, but the word "leather" was only in name, as the leather had been damaged by wind, snow, and moths, looking like water-stained cotton. Both cuffs were covered in grease like plaster. (114)

Brief News

Hong Jun, an antique enthusiast in the old capital, has moved his collection to Shanghai to avoid the turmoil. He has opened Shanlin at the intersection of Sanma Road and Guangxi Road. On the opening day, an exhibition was held, featuring exquisite bronzes, porcelains, calligraphy, paintings, and inkstones. There is a screen made of ivory and actual stones inlaid with the Four Beauties and Sixteen Sons, an ivory-inlaid jade rosewood cabinet, and eighteen tri-colored Arhats, all relics of the old palace. They are extremely precious. The calligraphy and paintings include landscapes by the renowned Qing painter, cursive scripts by Yang Jisheng, landscapes by Huang Shangu, and hand scrolls by Xinluo Shanren, Ruan Yuan, and Tang Yin. There are also a large number of Han jades, as red as blood, mostly well-known masterpieces from the old capital.

A Constant Business for Small Craftsmen and Small Capitalists

By Tianxu Wosheng

Recently, I have been asked for advice by many who are worried about unemployment and want to start small industrial businesses. I have been devising various plans to enable those who are currently unable to work to engage in a constant business in a short period of time, which can not only benefit themselves but also benefit others. In my opinion, the most stable option is to engage in the business of stationery and envelopes. With a deposit of only two hundred yuan, one can secure an exclusive area, without worrying about encroachment from latecomers. Even if one becomes tired of running the business and no longer wishes to continue, the original capital can still be recovered. Moreover, even if there is no business at all, one can still receive a monthly interest of one percent, providing some income. This is almost unparalleled in terms of capital stability. However, the method of allocation in terms of equipment should be as described below to avoid depletion.

㈠ For those who have no experience in stationery and envelope production, it is advisable to hire an experienced worker from a traditional paper shop, known as a "yi ba lian" worker. The so-called "yi ba lian" worker is capable of all four types of production: stationery, envelopes, notebooks, and ledgers, including printing, binding, and cutting. They are mostly apprentices who have become skilled workers. Printing only requires wooden blocks, paper cutting uses a drag knife, and ledger binding uses thread. All of these can be done without machines, but with some improvements to achieve machine-like printing. Paper shops can be asked to introduce such workers, and there will be no shortage of candidates. The monthly salary is generally from ten to sixteen yuan, and the cost of food and lodging will not exceed eighty cents per day. Taking letter paper as an example, the usual cost of sending it out to be printed is four jiao per thousand sheets. If one hires a worker to print it themselves, they can print an average of four thousand sheets per day, costing only two jiao per thousand sheets, which means one can earn eight jiao per day. After deducting pigments and consumables, one can earn at least twenty yuan per month. If two people work, they can earn forty yuan.

㈡ Wooden blocks can be carved locally at carving shops and do not necessarily require lead plates, as wooden blocks can also be printed with ink, producing the same quality as lead or stone printing. However, in the beginning, for the sake of the worker's familiarity, one can start with woodblock watermarking, which is already sufficient. Stationery can be distributed through ordinary eight-line businesses and sold by small shops on consignment. The procedure for ledgers is more complicated and is a good home-based industry. For example, workers can focus on printing and cutting, while folding and binding can be done by women and children. Envelopes can be sent out for lining, and workers can teach women and children how to fold them, which they will soon be able to do proficiently. If a family of five is originally idle, now each person can earn an average of two jiao per day, amounting to thirty yuan per month. Adding the worker's production, the surplus profit can also be twenty yuan, meaning that hiring only one person can yield a monthly income of fifty yuan. If one were to seek a monthly salary of fifty yuan elsewhere, it would be difficult to obtain and would be subject to loss because one would not have control, making it not a constant business. Therefore, one should encourage oneself with perseverance in this business to achieve success.

㈢ There are no restrictions on the type of paper used, but using paper that is larger in size and thicker in texture is more cost-effective than using ordinary Lianshi or Maobian paper. For example, ordinary Lianshi paper is 25 x 44, yielding only seven thousand 7 x 11 letter papers per ream. Liyong Lianshi paper is 28 x 44, yielding eight thousand sheets. When lining envelopes, two layers can be equivalent to three layers, twelve households can yield fifteen, fifteen households can yield eighteen, and eighteen households can yield twenty, and twenty-four households can yield twenty-eight, all of which are more than ordinary paper. When cutting, all yi ba lian workers can do it. The size of Liyong Maobian paper is also larger than ordinary paper, with ordinary paper being 25 x 52 and Liyong paper being 30 x 55. This is useful for making ledgers, allowing for a good fit without waste. (All the above dimensions are in inches.) Moreover, those who manage Liyong stationery and envelopes can return unused Liyong factory paper when purchasing it, making it more stable than any other industry.

㈣ The first month is entirely for preparation and production. To solicit orders from the outside, one can first purchase fifty or sixty yuan of Liyong office stationery and envelopes in stock, along with the original reams of paper as follows: (A) Five reams of 28 x 44 yuan-character Lianshi paper. (B) Five reams of 30 x 55 natural-color Maobian paper. (C) Two reams of 30 x 55 white Maobian paper. (D) Two reams of 30 x 44 lake-color newspaper. (E) Two reams of 28 x 44 Haiyue paper. The paper listed above is used for (A) printing stationery, (B) printing ledgers, (C) printing Ruyi stationery, and (D) and (E) lining envelopes, with two layers equivalent to three layers, or using two layers of (A) and one layer of (B). With the above allocation, one can have enough to work with. If there are any items with a specific brand name to be printed that one cannot print themselves, one can ask the Liyong office on the third floor of the Dalu Commercial Market to print them on their behalf, which should not be difficult.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly Summer Supplies and Consumer Psychology

By Yang Yan

The first priority for national goods factories is to cater to consumer psychology. If the products do not suit consumers' tastes, no matter how much you advertise or how cheap they are, they will not be very effective. The representative of consumers can be considered the housewife. Housewives hold the power of purchasing for most families. Therefore, it is better to cater to the psychology of general housewives than to cater to the psychology of consumers. Housewives are representatives of consumption, and all discerning housewives are constantly studying the trends of market products, material selection, and paying attention to the shifts in general psychology. Sometimes they have the task of guiding manufacturers to improve their products, and sometimes they have the task of guiding general consumers in their choices. Therefore, from the perspective of manufacturers, it is best to constantly pursue consumer psychology and keep up with it, without letting go in the slightest. Only then can products improve and sales be brisk. One day, I was chatting with Mr. Fang Yexian, and he said to an employee of the China National Goods Company, "I see that there are many women in the market wearing clothes with large floral patterns. We should pay attention to this." I admired these words from Mr. Fang because he was constantly using his mind to consider the psychology of general consumers. One day, the National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association, through the introduction of Mr. Zhang Yujiu, invited Mrs. Yu Yingjie to come and talk. Mrs. Yu is a housewife who is enthusiastic about national goods. She grew up in the United States and has lived in Shanghai for a long time. Throughout her life, she has been dedicated to the study of products and consumer psychology. The first thing she said was that the production of national goods must conform to consumer psychology. Remaining unchanged is the biggest taboo. Taking clothing as an example, Americans follow the French, always one step behind. For example, when large floral patterns are popular in the United States, striped patterns are already popular in France. If we do not study this, not to mention being behind in everything and having stagnant goods, how can we gain a foothold in the international market? She also said that the Chinese people think that cheap prices are the best they can do, but if the price is cheap but the material is not good, consumers will also turn away. In fact, some people do not care about cheap prices, but rather about durability and exquisiteness. She hoped that national goods factories would pay attention to this point and that shoddy production would ultimately fail. These words are truly golden rules.

I will now discuss summer supplies based on Mrs. Yu's words. Summer supplies boil down to six words: ㈠ Fashionable No matter what kind of product it is, the first priority is to be fashionable. Unfashionable products can only be placed in antique preservation societies as displays of antiques. Sometimes, putting them in the middle of other products will reduce the sales power of those products. Therefore, the first priority for manufacturers is to innovate and constantly study market trends, keep up with them, and avoid falling behind.

㈡ Color The second priority for summer supplies is color. Summer is hot, and the most taboo is eye-catching, glaring colors. Therefore, simple, elegant, and quiet colors are the most pleasing and the most popular.

㈢ Clever and Convenient Cleverness is an element of any product, but it is especially suitable for summer products. Summer rooms should be spacious, so the volume of items should not be bulky and take up space. Summer individuals should be light, so the style of items should not be cumbersome and difficult to carry. If you understand this point, you can win customers' welcome and consumers' satisfaction.

Therefore, we have published this special issue of summer national goods supplies. Many articles can be used as a reference for manufacturers and consumers. I hope everyone will provide practical guidance.

My Summer Supplies

By Hanmei

The god of summer has already spread its cruel wings and descended upon the world, expanding the authority of heat everywhere. Are humans, who are called the spirit of all things, relatively intelligent? I am reporting my daily necessities roughly:

Regarding Clothing

For long shirts and short shirts and pants, I chose China yarn produced by Sanyou Industrial Company, because of its fine and clean texture, soft and smooth against the skin, non-sticky when sweating, and very cheap price. When the weather is relatively cool, the long shirts I wear are also made of "Vienna" produced by Sanyou Company, because Vienna is elastic, does not wrinkle easily, and the color never fades. The undershirt is a Goose brand undershirt produced by Wuhe Weaving Factory, because it is durable and absorbs sweat most easily.

For Hats, I chose straw hats produced by Huafu Factory, Guanyi Factory, and Hefeng Factory, which are cheap, beautiful, and durable.

Regarding Bathing

For bath towels, I chose a No. 73 bath towel produced by Sanyou Company, which costs only 2 jiao and 9 fen per towel. After taking a cold water bath, I dry myself, which is very refreshing and comfortable, and can also be used as a small quilt at night.

The bath soap is medicated soap from Wuzhou Pharmacy, which functions to sterilize and disinfect, which is beneficial to hygiene.

After bathing, when enjoying the cool breeze and chatting, I was afraid of being affected by the wind and cold, so I went to Sanyou Company to buy a bathrobe to wear. Although the price is more than 2 yuan, after wearing it, it is not only convenient to put on and take off, but also very cool. It can be used as pajamas at night.

The back scrubber was also bought from Sanyou Company, because using a back scrubber when scrubbing your back makes it easier to remove dirt and save effort.

Regarding Bedding

Using a mosquito net is originally annoying, but mosquitoes are hateful, so I had to go to Sanyou Company to buy a sanitary mosquito net, which costs more than 6 yuan, but it is very cool and does not feel stuffy at all.

The sheets, thin quilts, and pillows are almost entirely handled by Sanyou Company. Others may say that you are doing free advertising for Sanyou Company, but no, Sanyou Company's goods are really very affordable and economical, and are national goods stores that are worthy of trust.

Regarding Other Items

Mosquito coils: I need to practice my homework at night, and the mosquitoes in the room are buzzing annoyingly, so the Samsung mosquito coils from China Chemical Industry Co. are almost like mosquito repellent envoys, and the mosquitoes will run away without being driven away.

Towels: Almost all Chinese people know the benefits of Triangle brand towels. I like to use them very much because they do not harden even after washing until they are broken.

Laundry soap: I use the Gubensao produced by Wuzhou Daye Pharmacy, because of its good quality and easy dirt removal, so we are very happy to use it.

From School to Society

I can confidently say that young people living in schools are the least able to understand the actual society thoroughly. This is because the essence of education is to transform society, not to adapt to it. The hearts of young people are pure, not base. However, actual society is invariably in contradiction and conflict with these ideals. This is perhaps acknowledged by some young people who have stepped into society.

Let me put aside my personal setbacks over the past two years and cite a few examples to discuss the lessons and understandings that society has given me.

With the intention of exchanging labor for a living, I accepted the position of a so-called private secretary. I thought it wouldn't be too bad or too contrary to the meaning of life. But the reality was different. My so-called employer was not genuinely dedicated to society and in need of a secretary's assistance. Instead, he was very wealthy and wanted to exploit the labor of others to elevate his own status. Because he felt his own efforts to ingratiate himself with society were insufficient. Thus, my heart was broken by him. I wrote articles for him with the goal of spreading his name in magazines and newspapers. The theory had to be moderate, and it was best to cite many wise words from contemporary celebrities, so that people in society would see that not only was his talent praiseworthy, but his writing was also excellent. I wrote letters for him, which he prepared to use as a stepping stone to request studying abroad. He often said: "With writings, and with more relationships in various aspects, there will be a way. You work hard, and there will be substantial rewards in the future!" This meant that studying and writing articles were for building "connections" and elevating one's personal social status. When I was in school, I never dreamed of this. I only knew that the purpose of studying and the intention of writing were to solve my own livelihood from the intention of contributing to society and seeking the welfare of the public. That was enough.

Once, I went to X City to find a friend to seek employment. Upon meeting, my friend said: "You want to find a job? How is your mouth? If you can't boast a few skills, relying solely on so-called ability or a friend's recommendation won't work!" Utterly naive, I didn't pay much attention at the time, thinking he was just joking. Knowing he was a resourceful friend, I still stayed without much concern. He introduced me once, twice, three times. I stayed for ten days, half a month, a month. The result was constant setbacks, without any progress. At the same time, I saw others succeed within a few days after a single introduction. So my friend said: "That person knows how to talk, knows how to praise, and has a certain relationship, a certain 'historical background.'" Only then did I realize something. I rolled up my bedding and said goodbye to my friend: "I'll go back for now!" "Okay, go work on your writing. We'll talk again when there's an opportunity!" Heaven knows, is this something I ever dreamed of in school? Even with a brain full of talent and a bachelor's degree, where can I auction it off?

Another time, I returned to my hometown of X X, and a few friends gathered to discuss starting a weekly newspaper. Some advocated pulling strings and finding a backstage boss, while others strongly argued for creating a name first before accepting any self-sought backing or subsidies. The ultimate purpose of starting the newspaper was to lay a foundation in X X. This was another base and filthy farce, never imagined when running a wall newspaper or society journal in school. But my friends said with experience that if it wasn't done this way, there was no point in doing it at all. If you want to promote culture, the social environment will not allow it. So, like a fleeting flower, it vanished in a few days.

From these few extremely ordinary facts, the following conclusions can be drawn:

(1) Education does not transform society. The resounding words in the teacher's mouth and the truths in the textbook can only assist you in going in the opposite direction, and cannot be truly applied to actual society.

(2) If you want to survive in society, you must "adapt." If someone says "yes," you must follow up with a "right." If someone is higher than you, you must flatter them. If someone is lower than you, you might as well lord over them and treat them like a lapdog. You must master the art of "blowing" and "flattering." When you do things, only consider whether it benefits yourself, whether it can solidify your own position, and expand your own influence. You must wring out the purity of your heart and set aside the truths and beliefs in the textbooks.

This terrible real society!

Clerk's Communication: I Want to Change Customs

Editor:

I am a young man in my twenties, and I have never been involved in any major events. Today, I am requesting your help in resolving a difficult issue, namely marriage. Four years ago, through the words of a matchmaker, I became engaged to a traditional woman. Recently, I received a letter from my hometown stating that the wedding date has been chosen. According to the customs of my hometown, the wedding procedures are very troublesome and costly, which I personally strongly disagree with. I intend to use the newest and simplest form of marriage, eliminating all the procedures. I am afraid that my uncles and the woman's family will oppose this. How should I deal with them? Please help me think of the most appropriate and simplest solution!

Respectfully, Wang Jiwei

××××

Editor's Note: The traditional wedding procedures are indeed troublesome and costly. Wang's proposal for reform is not without merit. However, in life, unless it concerns one's own vital interests, one should not necessarily stubbornly cling to one's own views. Other matters of minor importance should perhaps not be held onto so rigidly. For example, at the time of the wedding, if it is within one's means, spending a little more money is not a big deal. We who study economic issues should focus on the entire society. If I spend a little more money today, this money will still circulate in society! Moreover, once a new family is formed (the bride), they will inevitably need to buy some new furniture, so it is not necessarily a waste. Even if some old-fashioned customs are used, the cost is not very high, and it has no relation to the marriage itself. If one stubbornly insists on one's own views, causing rifts in various relationships, it is probably not worth it. Therefore, this matter should be handled with consideration within the limits of one's financial ability and without harming relationships. Excessive spending is certainly not right, but being too stubborn is also unnecessary.

He raised his head, took a breath of fresh air, and then walked victoriously towards Chen's mansion.

Reaching the gate of the mansion, he re-examined the grand speech he had prepared. After pressing the doorbell, the servant opened the door a crack, as if afraid that an uninvited guest would suddenly rush in. He first sized up Shi Qiao's attire, and then said:

"Your card, I'll go see if Commissioner Chen is home?" The servants always liked to call out the master's official title. Even a commander-in-chief who had been dismissed for several years was still called "Commander So-and-So" by everyone. After he went in, Shi Qiao's heart started to beat faster. He couldn't tell whether it was cowardice or excessive excitement.

Scholarship Rules 184

Article 1: The Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Institute, in order to assist impoverished, honest, and ambitious young people in pursuing further education, establishes scholarships.

Article 2: The amount of the scholarship shall be determined by the board of directors based on the financial situation of the institute.

Article 3: The institute, in order to handle scholarship matters, may appoint a committee of several people, organized by the chairman of the board of directors, to handle them.

Article 4: Any organization or individual donating over five thousand yuan to the institute for scholarships shall be a natural member of the Scholarship Fund Committee. The organization may nominate one person as a representative.

Article 5: Any organization or individual donating over twenty thousand yuan to the institute for scholarships may have their name or surname prefixed to the scholarship, named the "So-and-so Scholarship," and shall be a natural member of the Scholarship Fund Committee. The organization may nominate one person as a representative.

Article 6: All scholarships issued by the institute, except as stipulated in the preceding article, shall be called the "Zhongshan Scholarship."

Article 7: Students to be assisted by the institute shall, for the time being, be limited to graduates of domestic junior and senior high schools and undergraduates who have passed the institute's various examinations, and who have a guarantor to prove that they are indeed impoverished, honest, and ambitious.

Article 8: The school and subject of study of students receiving assistance must be determined with the consent of the institute.

Article 9: Students receiving assistance who drop out of school midway without the permission of the institute shall be required to return the scholarship amount received.

Article 10: Students receiving assistance whose academic performance or conduct is poor, as reported by the school or otherwise proven, may have their scholarship amount suspended or recovered at any time.

Article 11: Students receiving assistance shall keep a daily diary and report in detail to the institute each semester on what they have learned at school for examination.

Article 12: After graduating from the school, students receiving assistance may be recruited by the institute for service for a mandatory period of one year.

Article 13: Regulations for the organization of various committees and the examination of scholarship students shall be determined separately.

Article 14: Matters not fully covered in these rules may be amended at any time.

Article 15: These rules shall be implemented upon approval by the board of directors.

(Resolution) To request the headquarters to promptly issue various registration forms and regulations. ㈥ How to reorganize the various groups in the city in preparation for participating in the National Revitalization Grand Review. (Resolution) To be handled jointly by the guidance and assessment sections. ㈦ Secretary Luo presented a proposal that the work plans of the guidance and compilation sections, which had been submitted to the meeting for review, were in order and should be approved. (Resolution) Approved. ㈧ The assessment section submitted a draft work plan for modification and approval. (Resolution) Approved with modifications. ㈨ Executive Council Member Tong Xingbai proposed that, for the sake of the association's affairs, Council Member Wang Gang should be authorized to act on behalf of his executive position, with Council Member Tong still bearing the responsibility. (Resolution) Approved. ㈩ The association's current residence is about to expire, and it is urgently necessary to relocate. How should this be handled? (Resolution) To be handled by the Executive Council. To submit a proposal to the headquarters to forward it to the Ministry of Railways, requesting a revision of the preferential treatment measures for Boy Scouts traveling by train. (Resolution) Approved.

Shanghai County Education Association Holds Third Delegates' Congress 186

▲ Sun Jichu and Six Others Elected as Directors

▲ Organize Guidance for Primary and Secondary School Admissions and Employment

The first meeting of the third session of the Shanghai County Education Association was held yesterday at the Xin Zhi County Party Headquarters to elect directors and discuss important proposals. Details are as follows:

▲ Participating delegates included Zhu Jiasheng and Yu Zuobin from the First District, Ding Hanzhang and Li Youtian from the Second District, Sun Jichu and Zhang Yi from the Third District, and Sun Zhixing and Zhang from the Sixth District. Absent were Ding Renke and Zhou Yuanliang. Also present were County Magistrate Zeng Zhenfei, Education Bureau Chief Shi She, Education Committee Member Lin Qing, County Party Headquarters Representatives Chen Jiapu and Yang Youyun, and Directors Ma Yiwen, Zheng Guozhai, Shi Qiyuan, and Xu Pengcheng.

▲ Meeting Details: Delegates registered at 10:00 AM. The delegates' oath ceremony was held at 10:30 AM, presided over by Chairman Bi Huan, County Magistrate Cao Zhenfei, and Education Bureau Chief Shi She. After the oath ceremony, a preliminary meeting was held, chaired by Zhang. Zhang was immediately elected as the chairman of the congress, and Zhu Jiasheng and Zhang were appointed as members of the congress declaration drafting committee. At 11:40 AM, the proposal review committee was held. The official meeting began at 1:50 PM with eight delegates present, chaired by Zhang, recorded by Xu Pengcheng, and the ceremony conducted by Wang Daoming. First, the chairman delivered the opening remarks, followed by a report on the association's affairs by the executive directors. Representatives from the County Party Headquarters, Chen Jiapu, the County Government, Bi Huan, and the County Education Bureau, Shi She, then delivered speeches. Next, directors were elected and proposals were discussed. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM with a group photo and slogans.

▲ Directors Election: The double-anonymous consecutive voting method was used, with Jin Zuobin distributing ballots, Zhang Yi supervising the voting, Sun Zhongli counting ballots, and Li Youtian recording ballots. As a result, Sun Jichu, Zhang Zhuo, Li Youtian, Chen Chen, Ding Renke, Zhang Yi, and Jin Zuobin were elected as directors. Zhu Jiasheng, Zheng Yi, and Ding Hongzhang were elected as alternate directors.

▲ Discussion of Proposals: ㈠ Amendment of the Articles of Association. Resolved: The original articles were passed. ㈡ Organizing guidance for primary and secondary school admissions and employment. Resolved: The board of directors will formulate measures and submit them to the Education Bureau for implementation. ㈢ Organizing a research association. Resolved: Passed. The board of directors will plan and implement it. ㈣ Requesting the Education Association to subsidize the district education associations' allowances. Resolved: 1. The association has no legal basis to subsidize the district education associations. 2. District education associations should request subsidies from local autonomous bodies when necessary. ㈤ Requesting the County Education Bureau to appropriately increase primary school teachers' salaries starting from next year. Resolved: Passed. ㈥ Publishing publications to promote and popularize education. Resolved: To be handled by the board of directors. ㈦ Submitting a request to the county government for financial assistance. Resolved: To be handled by the board of directors. ㈧ Reducing the budget for rural primary school tuition fees. Resolved: To be handled by the board of directors. ㈨ Unifying the membership fees of the association's district branches. Resolved: The entrance fee is set at 30 cents, and the annual fee is set at 40 cents, to be handled by the board of directors. ㈩ Requesting supervisors and education commissioners to provide model teaching by district. Resolved: Passed. ㈩㈠ Whether the association should express condolences for the passing of former association president Mr. Wang Yincai due to illness. Resolved: Zhang Yi and Zhang will be sent to pay respects.

British Tobacco Factory Suddenly Orders the Recovery of Workers' Children's School 192

▲ Union Representatives Petition Party and Government Agencies

▲ Demand that the Factory Fulfill the Labor-Management Contract

The Pudong British-American Workers' Children's School was established in 1928. On April 1, 1929, the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs, together with labor and management, signed a labor-management contract stipulating that the factory would be happy to subsidize the school's expenses. At that time, the factory provided a monthly subsidy of 1,500 yuan. At that time, there were only over 300 students. Now it has grown to over 600 students, but the factory subsidy has been reduced to 750 yuan, which has limited the school's administration and made it impossible to develop economically. The school plans to hire educators as trustees starting next semester to seek improvements. However, the factory suddenly used poor management as an excuse and insisted on taking it back. The union was surprised to hear this and has sent representative Chen Peide to petition the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs, demanding that the factory fulfill the contract. The result was very satisfactory.

National Games Preparatory Committee 195

Sports Association Plans to Launch Chinese Baseball League 196

▲ But Schools on Vacation May Make It Difficult to Realize

The National Sports Federation, in view of the fact that baseball in Shanghai is about to disappear, has no choice but to promote and revitalize it. It has contacted universities such as St. John's, Fudan, and Jiaotong to launch the Shanghai Chinese Baseball League Championship this summer. It has dismantled the west side of the baseball field's grandstand and the wire mesh to create a ground for baseball games. However, as it is the summer vacation and schools are on break, most of the students are scattered, and it may be difficult to organize teams. Therefore, the Sports Federation's plan may be difficult to realize. If a dedicated team is formed, there will be no opponents to compete against. Western teams are too strong, making it impossible to win. And a league competition may be difficult to achieve. Promoting baseball is also difficult. It is hoped that all schools will organize teams to participate and work together to revitalize baseball.

Hong Kong Western Football Club Revises Rules 197

▲ Those Not Residing Within the Jurisdiction May Not Participate in Competitions

In recent years, many players from the Hong Kong South China and Chinese football clubs have been serving in Guangzhou. When South China and China have important games, they go to Hong Kong to participate in the war. The Hong Kong Western Football Club is concerned that this kind of round-trip game will cause difficulties in future inter-port competitions. Therefore, it was specially discussed at the meeting on the 14th of this month, and it was resolved that players who do not reside within the jurisdiction of Hong Kong and Kowloon may not participate in the competition. This is very unfavorable to the South China and China clubs.

Lawn Tennis League

Greater Hope for Championship: Chinese Tennis Club Defeats Japanese Spinning Factory 200

▲ Result: 11 to 4, Second, Third, and Fourth Groups Win Completely

▲ First Group Loses One Point in a Dramatic Battle, Fifth Group Loses Completely

In yesterday's lawn tennis league match between the Chinese Club and the powerful Japanese Internal and External Spinning Factory, the location was inside the Japanese Spinning Factory at the intersection of Robert Road and Jiaozhou Road. The Chinese Club and the Japanese Spinning Factory each defeated the Japanese Club with a score of 10 to 5. Therefore, yesterday's battle was thought to be very intense. But as a result, the Chinese Club won by a score of 11 to 4. Thus, the Chinese Club's hope for the championship is becoming more and more stable. The results of each group are as follows:

㈠ Lin Maihua Zheng Zhaojia {7丨9 7丨5 6丨1} Machida Koji (Japan)

㈡ Qiu Feihai Xian Yaobin {6丨0 6丨3 6丨2} Tsukiji Kamata (Japan)

㈢ Yu Tianguang Liang Deguang {6丨2 7丨5 7丨5} Sakane Imai (Japan)

㈣ Tu Kaiyuan Sun Linfang {6丨4 6丨3 6丨4} Ishii Kamimura (Japan)

㈤ Zheng Zirong Zhou Huafu {6丨8 3丨6 8丨10} Yamamoto Kobayashi (Japan)

Dramatic Battle in the First Group 201

Yesterday, the first group, Lin and Zheng, because they were too careful, made their arms weak and nervous, and the ball situation got worse and worse, resulting in a 7 to 9 loss in the first set. Japanese players Machida and Koji attacked behind Lin and Zheng with high balls, giving them no chance to counterattack. Lin and Zheng were in a very difficult situation and could only return with high balls, but with little accuracy, either going out of bounds or near the net, where they were subject to the opponent's fierce attacks. In the first set, Lin and Zheng were trapped in this situation and were at a loss. In addition, the two were less energetic yesterday than they had been in the previous battle against the Japanese Club, and they were like two different people. Lin and Zheng lost 1 to 4 first, then chased to 5 to 5, but the following priorities were all taken by the opponent, resulting in a final loss of 7 to 9. In the second set, Lin and Zheng won 5 to 3, thinking it would be easy to win, but unexpectedly it became 5 to 5 again, and they won 7 to 5, which was worrying. In the third set, Lin and Zheng's momentum was stronger and slightly better, ending with 6 to 1.

Complete Defeat in the Fifth Group 202

The complete defeat in the fifth set cost China three points. If they could have taken one or two, the total score would have been even more impressive. Zheng Zirong and Zhou Huafu, who played, lacked stability, and because of their age, they had no heroic spirit. As a result, they lost 6 to 8, 3 to 6, and 8 to 10 completely.

Complete Victory in the Remaining Three Groups 203

The second group, Qiu Feihai and Qian Yaobin, finished the earliest. Their opponents, Tsukiji and Kamata, had average skills and could not withstand Qiu and Qian's fierce attacks. As a result of the three sets, Qiu and Qian lost only five of the total twenty-three games, which can be said to be extremely easy. The next to finish was the third group, Yu Tianguang and Liang Deguang. In the first set, Yu and Liang won 6 to 2 very easily. The situation in the following two sets was tense, but Yu and Liang won 7 to 5 in a row. The next to finish was the fifth group, Tu Kaiyuan and Sun Linfang, who also won in three straight sets. The three groups won a total of nine points, and China won in a triumphant manner with a score of 11 to 4.

Great Hope for China 204

In the Group A lawn tennis league, China has played five times, winning 58 of 75 sets and losing only 17 sets, which is unmatched. All strong opponents such as Portugal, the Japanese Club, the Japanese Spinning Factory, South Lawn, and North Lawn have been defeated. The remaining three teams, the French Chamber of Commerce, the Xieqiao General Association, and the Citibank Country Association, are all of average strength. Therefore, China is almost certain to win the championship.
